-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Absorb                                                   *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Ward Spells -- Einvigi and Baldursvorn                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Two Tier-4 ward spells provide percentage absorb         *~-
-~*  against incoming damage.  Each absorbs a fixed           *~-
-~*  rate of qualifying hits until its duration runs out.     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  HOW WARDS WORK                                           *~-
-~*  A ward absorbs a set % of each qualifying hit.           *~-
-~*  The rate is fixed on cast (stat-scaled, max 88%).        *~-
-~*  Duration ticks down by 1 for each absorbed hit           *~-
-~*  AND by 1 each heartbeat.  When duration reaches          *~-
-~*  zero the ward expires.                                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EINVIGI                                                  *~-
-~*  Tyr, T4. Absorbs physical (edged/blunt) only.            *~-
-~*  BALDURSVORN                                              *~-
-~*  Baldr, T4. Absorbs elemental, poison, mind,              *~-
-~*  and radiation.                                           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  The two wards stack -- cast both for full coverage.      *~-
-~*  Toggle brief_ward suppresses per-hit messages.           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read this topic top-to-bottom once.                   *~-
-~*  2) Apply the related commands in small steps.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck this topic as your setup evolves.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Most issues come from skipped prerequisites.             *~-
-~*  If behavior differs, verify stats, toggles, resources.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vhelp combat/absorb                                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vcast, vtoggle                                 *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Chains                                                   *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Melee Combat Chain System                                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Openers begin a chain; follow-up strikes build from      *~-
-~*  the prior round.  Chains grow with skill investment.     *~-
-~*  Changing targets resets the current chain.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMBAT TAGS                                              *~-
-~*  Openers leave markers that shape which strikes can       *~-
-~*  follow on the next round.  Multiple tags can stack.      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  BODY STRIKES                                             *~-
-~*  Body strikes form a parallel chain system layered on     *~-
-~*  top of melee combat.  They have their own chain depth    *~-
-~*  and technique categories and are developed separately.   *~-
-~*  Use vstrike to see your current mastery status.          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  RELEVANT SKILLS                                          *~-
-~*  Several skills in the Viga path interact with chains.    *~-
-~*  Use vhelp skills <skill> for details.                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read this topic top-to-bottom once.                   *~-
-~*  2) Apply the related commands in small steps.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck this topic as your setup evolves.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Most issues come from skipped prerequisites.             *~-
-~*  If behavior differs, verify stats, toggles, resources.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vhelp combat/chains                                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vstrike, vskills                               *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Hird                                                     *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Hirdmadr -- Recruitable Combat Guards                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Certain subclasses can recruit named hirdmadrs to        *~-
-~*  fight alongside them in battle.  They gain experience    *~-
-~*  through kills and grow in ability over time.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  HOW THE FLOW WORKS                                       *~-
-~*  Recruits enter your hird pool first (vhird). From there  *~-
-~*  you choose where they serve:                             *~-
-~*  personal guard, city garrison,                           *~-
-~*  or longship crews.                                       *~-
-~*  Use vguard to muster named                               *~-
-~*  guards to your side. Use vhird                           *~-
-~*  for pool management and assignment into garrison/ships.  *~-
-~*  Mustered guards return to your                           *~-
-~*  pool when stood down or when                             *~-
-~*  they are no longer active in your guard formation.       *~-
-~*  Guards wounded in battle recover automatically after a   *~-
-~*  cooldown. When the timer expires they re-muster to your  *~-
-~*  side without needing a manual vguard muster.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  PERSONAL GUARD (vguard)                                  *~-
-~*  Muster named hirdmadrs to fight with you.  Guard cap     *~-
-~*  scales with your skill investment in Vegr Hersins.       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  GUARD ABILITIES                                          *~-
-~*  Some Hersins skills unlock abilities your guards can     *~-
-~*  use in battle alongside you.                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  GARRISON AND SHIPS                                       *~-
-~*  Hirdmadrs can also staff your city garrison or crew      *~-
-~*  your longships during raids.                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read this topic top-to-bottom once.                   *~-
-~*  2) Apply the related commands in small steps.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck this topic as your setup evolves.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Most issues come from skipped prerequisites.             *~-
-~*  If behavior differs, verify stats, toggles, resources.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vhelp combat/hird                                        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vguard, vhird                                  *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Spellcasting                                             *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  The Seer Spell System                                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Seers channel Seid to cast spells granted by their       *~-
-~*  patron god.  Devotion deepens with use, unlocking        *~-
-~*  more of what a god can offer over time.                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  SPELL TIERS                                              *~-
-~*  Each god grants spells in tiers.  Higher tiers are       *~-
-~*  earned through long dedication to a single patron.       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  CAST TYPES                                               *~-
-~*  Instant      Fires in the same beat as vcast.            *~-
-~*  Channeled    Resolves over time; effect on completion.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  AUTOCAST SLOTS                                           *~-
-~*  Only a limited number of spells can be active at         *~-
-~*  once.  Slot limits vary by spell category.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  DEVOTION SCALING                                         *~-
-~*  Spell power grows as you cast more and your bond         *~-
-~*  with your patron deepens.                                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read this topic top-to-bottom once.                   *~-
-~*  2) Apply the related commands in small steps.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck this topic as your setup evolves.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Most issues come from skipped prerequisites.             *~-
-~*  If behavior differs, verify stats, toggles, resources.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vhelp combat/spells                                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vcast, vgod                                    *~-

-~*  Spells                                                   *~-

-~*  Hp                                                       *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: hp                                                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Displays your current HP, SP, and any relevant           *~-
-~*  recovery or combat status indicators.                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Use vsethp to customise which values are shown.          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) hp for quick current combat/resource state.           *~-
-~*  2) vsethp to adjust displayed fields/order.              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  hp                                                       *~-
-~*  vsethp                                                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Invalid syntax or context can block action.              *~-
-~*  Check syntax here and retry.                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vsethp, vstrike, vstats, vscore                *~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Mip                                                      *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vmip                                              *~-
-~*  vtoggle mip_extra                                        *~-
-~*  vtoggle mip_city                                         *~-
-~*  vtoggle mip_trade_goods                                  *~-
-~*  vtoggle mip_map                                          *~-
-~*  vtoggle mip_voyage                                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Controls Viking live data feeds used by MIP-aware        *~-
-~*  clients and custom plugins.  Feeds are sent each         *~-
-~*  heartbeat and can be toggled independently.              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  WHAT YOU RECEIVE                                         *~-
-~*  Base combat channels (always available to MIP):          *~-
-~*  GP1 current/max = Fury, GLINE1 = vitals bar text,        *~-
-~*  GLINE2 = saga/enemy line text.                           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  mip_extra (sub-code 225, KEY~value pairs): all           *~-
-~*  guild_hp_map values with ANSI removed and 0/empty        *~-
-~*  values omitted.  Includes hp resources, fury/chain,      *~-
-~*  saga/gxp, ledung, enemy text, spell effects, and         *~-
-~*  other status tokens used by guild displays.              *~-
-~*  Also includes GOD_POWER, GOD_POWER_NEXT, and             *~-
-~*  GOD_POWER_FOCUS for rotating god-power state.            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  mip_city (sub-code 225, KEY~value pairs): CARTS,         *~-
-~*  CIDLE, CUPG, SHIPS, WSTOCK, BLOT, FARM, BUILDS,          *~-
-~*  SUPG, GARRISON, THRALLS, MISSIONS, ERRAND, BDMG,         *~-
-~*  STAFF, HIRD, WEATHER, NEXTTICK, DCYCLE, MARKET,          *~-
-~*  INCOMING, plus map keys VMAPH, VMAPL, VMR## rows.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  CARTS KEY (part of mip_city)                             *~-
-~*  CARTS:                                                   *~-
-~*  mode|good|village|secs|amt|half_in|quality_pct|cart_id|  *~-
-~*  tier|durability|cap;...                                  *~-
-~*  Active (dispatched) trade carts. Semicolon-separated.    *~-
-~*  Fields: mode (buy/sell), good,                           *~-
-~*  village, seconds remaining,                              *~-
-~*  amount, halfway seconds, quality pct, cart_id (1-N),     *~-
-~*  tier (1-5), durability (0-100), capacity (units).        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  CIDLE KEY (part of mip_city)                             *~-
-~*  CIDLE: cart_id|tier|durability|cap;...                   *~-
-~*  Idle carts not currently                                 *~-
-~*  dispatched. Semicolon-separated.                         *~-
-~*  Fields: cart_id (1-N), tier (1-5), durability (0-100),   *~-
-~*  capacity (effective units for this cart).                *~-
-~*  Use to show docked/available carts in your UI.           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  FARM KEY (part of mip_city)                              *~-
-~*  FARM:                                                    *~-
-~*  coord|shroom_id|time_left|fertilized|wilt_left;...       *~-
-~*  Mushroom farm plots. Multiple                            *~-
-~*  plots separated by semicolon.                            *~-
-~*  Fields: coord (A1, B2, etc.),                            *~-
-~*  shroom_id, seconds until ready,                          *~-
-~*  fertilized flag (0/1), wilt_left (-1=growing,            *~-
-~*  0=wilted, >0=seconds to wilt).                           *~-
-~*  time_left=0 means READY. First entry                     *~-
-~*  is always meta|weather_mod.                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  SETTLER KEYS (part of mip_city)                          *~-
-~*  SETTLERS: population|tax|water|mood                      *~-
-~*  Basic settler summary (legacy, always included).         *~-
-~*  SETTLERX: mood|security|dignity|flourishing|jobs|        *~-
-~*  employed|market_staffed|housing_cap|housing_plots|       *~-
-~*  housing_avg|housing_upkeep|community_upkeep|net          *~-
-~*  Full governance snapshot each tick.                      *~-
-~*  housing_avg is x100 (divide by 100 for tier float).      *~-
-~*  net is the signed settler_community_net/tick value.      *~-
-~*  SACTIONS: id|timer|cooldown;id|timer|cooldown;...        *~-
-~*  One entry per community action.  timer=0 means           *~-
-~*  the action is not currently active; cooldown=0           *~-
-~*  means it is available to trigger.                        *~-
-~*  SPROJ: kind|target_tier|secs_remaining;...               *~-
-~*  Pending settler construction projects in the queue.      *~-
-~*  kind is 'housing' or a community building id.            *~-
-~*  secs_remaining counts down to auto-completion.           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  mip_trade_goods (sub-code 225): TGOODS compact           *~-
-~*  demand/supply by lineage and good.  Neutral entries      *~-
-~*  are omitted for packet size.                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  mip_map (sub-code 225): full territory payload with      *~-
-~*  VMAPH header, VMAPL POI list, VMR## terrain rows,        *~-
-~*  and path graph edges MEE##/MES## for click-move UIs.     *~-
-~*  This feed is large and off by default.                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  mip_voyage (sub-code 225): voyage status, chart tiles,   *~-
-~*  ship info, and voyage log updates. Sent whenever voyage  *~-
-~*  state changes (launch, move, node resolution, harbor).   *~-
-~*  Includes SHIP_DATA, VOYAGE_STATE, CHART_TILES, and       *~-
-~*  pending contract info for voyage UIs.                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  FORMAT NOTES FOR PLUGIN AUTHORS                          *~-
-~*  Packet format is KEY~VALUE~KEY~VALUE.  Array values      *~-
-~*  use semicolon-separated entries with pipe-separated      *~-
-~*  fields inside each entry.  Map rows are plain symbol     *~-
-~*  strings.  Long payloads may arrive chunked, so merge     *~-
-~*  updates by key instead of assuming one packet has all.   *~-
-~*  Delimiters ~ and ^ are sanitized before map rows send.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  PARSING EXAMPLE                                          *~-
-~*  Example packet fragment:                                 *~-
-~*  SETTLERS~420|2|185|78~                                   *~-
-~*  SETTLERX~78|62|55|0|140|118|4|480|12|225|30|20|5~        *~-
-~*  SACTIONS~feast|0|3600;workdrive|0|0~                     *~-
-~*  SPROJ~housing|2|1420;market|3|870~                       *~-
-~*  VMAPH~41|24|18|9~                                        *~-
-~*  CARTS~sell|timber|Austerfall|420|12|210|100|1|2|85|37;.  *~-
-~*  ..~                                                      *~-
-~*  CIDLE~2|1|100|30;3|3|70|45~                              *~-
-~*  Decode steps: split on ~ into key/value pairs,           *~-
-~*  route by key, then parse list values with ; and |.       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Recommended: start with mip_extra+mip_city, then add     *~-
-~*  mip_trade_goods, mip_map, or mip_voyage                  *~-
-~*  only when your UI needs it.                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Enable mip_extra and mip_city first.                  *~-
-~*  2) Build parser support for KEY~VALUE packet pairs.      *~-
-~*  3) Use SETTLERX, SACTIONS, SPROJ for settler UI panels.  *~-
-~*  4) Add mip_trade_goods, mip_map, or                      *~-
-~*  mip_voyage only when required.                           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Broken parsing usually comes from delimiter handling.    *~-
-~*  If settler UI seems stale, check SETTLERX is parsed      *~-
-~*  separately from SETTLERS; they are different keys.       *~-
-~*  Merge chunked packets by key before rendering.           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vtoggle mip_extra                                        *~-
-~*  vtoggle mip_city                                         *~-
-~*  vtoggle mip_trade_goods                                  *~-
-~*  vtoggle mip_map                                          *~-
-~*  vtoggle mip_voyage                                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vtoggle, vstats, vcity                         *~-
-~*  vsettler, vbuild, vvoyage                                *~-

-~*                                                           *~-

-~*  the current recovery rate.                               *~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Vansi                                                    *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vansi show                                        *~-
-~*  vansi default                                            *~-
-~*  vansi set <role> <colour>                                *~-
-~*  vansi preset <classic|highcontrast>                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Manage guild-specific ANSI colour variables.             *~-
-~*  Theme roles cover borders, headers, subheaders,          *~-
-~*  body text, and command/example text.                     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  show         list all variables and current colours      *~-
-~*  default      reset all variables to guild defaults       *~-
-~*  set          set one role: border, header,               *~-
-~*               subheader, body, command                    *~-
-~*  preset       apply a bundled theme quickly               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vansi show to inspect current role colours.           *~-
-~*  2) vansi set <role> <colour> for targeted changes.       *~-
-~*  3) vansi preset or vansi default to normalize theme.     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Unknown role/colour values: use vansi show guidance.     *~-
-~*  Unreadable mix: reset with vansi default or preset.      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vansi show                                               *~-
-~*  vansi set border blue                                    *~-
-~*  vansi preset highcontrast                                *~-
-~*  vansi default                                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Examples: vansi set border blue                          *~-
-~*  vansi set body white                                     *~-
-~*  vansi preset highcontrast                                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Raw aset still works for individual viking_* vars.       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vtoggle, vsethp                                *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Varmour                                                  *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: varmour                                           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Displays your armour mastery levels per slot and         *~-
-~*  progress toward the next level.  Mastery grows by        *~-
-~*  taking hits in combat while wearing each slot.           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Slots: Helmet, Armour, Breastplate, Greaves,             *~-
-~*  Gloves, Boots, Cloak, Shield.                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Higher mastery amplifies the AC absorption your          *~-
-~*  worn armour already provides on each hit.                *~-
-~*  Cap: level 50 per slot.                                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Admins: varmour <player> views another Viking.           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) varmour to inspect per-slot progression.              *~-
-~*  2) Wear target slots consistently during combat.         *~-
-~*  3) Recheck growth and balance weaker slots.              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Slow progression usually means slot not equipped often.  *~-
-~*  No gain when taking no meaningful absorbed hits.         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  varmour                                                  *~-
-~*  varmour skuggis                                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vstats                                         *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vavenge                                           *~-

-~*  Mark a player as your target for vengeance after         *~-
-~*  being killed.  Tracks outstanding debts of honour.       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vavenge after a hostile death to review targets.      *~-
-~*  2) Track and settle marked grudges over time.            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  No valid recent aggressor means no new mark is added.    *~-
-~*  Cleared grudges no longer appear in active listings.     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Vban                                                     *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vban                                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Apply or clear Viking restriction flags on players.      *~-
-~*  Restrictions can target chat, gxp, guild joining,        *~-
-~*  and guild leaving, with timed or permanent duration.     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  PERMISSION TIERS                                         *~-
-~*  Guild Admin: chat restrictions                           *~-
-~*  Guild Wizard: gxp restrictions                           *~-
-~*  Allgodi: join, leave, or all restrictions                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vban show <player> to inspect current restrictions.   *~-
-~*  2) vban <player> <flags>                                 *~-
-~*  <duration|perm> [reason] to apply.                       *~-
-~*  3) vban clear <player> <flags|all> [reason] to remove.   *~-
-~*  4) vban list to review all active restrictions.          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Using a flag above your rank is denied explicitly.       *~-
-~*  Use min for minutes and m for                            *~-
-~*  months in timed durations.                               *~-
-~*  Join/leave restrictions are reserved for Allgodi.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vban loch chat 2h channel abuse                          *~-
-~*  vban loch gxp 1d exploit investigation                   *~-
-~*  vban loch join,leave perm guild ban                      *~-
-~*  vban clear loch chat appeal accepted                     *~-
-~*  vban show loch                                           *~-
-~*  vban list                                                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vbug, vhelp, vik, vrecommend                   *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*  Vbuild                                                   *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vbuild                                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Build structures in your city.  Available buildings      *~-
-~*  depend on your skill investment and current city         *~-
-~*  tier.  Use vbuild alone to see current options.          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  SUBCOMMANDS                                              *~-
-~*  list         List all buildings with                     *~-
-~*               costs and descriptions.                     *~-
-~*  status       Show current buildings                      *~-
-~*               and production rates.                       *~-
-~*  info <bld>   Detailed tier breakdown for one building.   *~-
-~*  start <bld>  Build or upgrade to next tier.              *~-
-~*  cancel <bld>  Cancel active construction.                *~-
-~*  demolish <bld>  Destroy a building (no refund).          *~-
-~*  repair <bld>  Repair structural damage.                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vbuild to review current city state.                  *~-
-~*  2) vbuild list to compare building costs and tiers.      *~-
-~*  3) vbuild start <name> to begin a build or upgrade.      *~-
-~*  4) vbuild status to track delivery and completion.       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Unknown building: run vbuild list for valid names.       *~-
-~*  Insufficient daler: earn more before you start.          *~-
-~*  Missing prerequisite: build dependencies first.          *~-
-~*  Cancel warning: materials return; spent daler does not.  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vbuild list                                              *~-
-~*  vbuild start warehouse                                   *~-
-~*  vbuild start smithy                                      *~-
-~*  vbuild status                                            *~-
-~*  vbuild cancel smithy                                     *~-
-~*  vbuild demolish fishery                                  *~-
-~*  vbuild repair lumber_yard                                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vcity, vskills                                 *~-

-~*  Vdash                                                    *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vdash                                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  A customizable dashboard showing individual Viking       *~-
-~*  guild data items. Pick exactly what you want to see.     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  SUBCOMMANDS                                              *~-
-~*  add <item>   Add a data item to your dashboard.          *~-
-~*  remove <item>  Remove an item from your dashboard.       *~-
-~*  order <items>  Reorder all items at once.                *~-
-~*  list         List available items and                    *~-
-~*               your current layout.                        *~-
-~*  reset        Reset to default layout.                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  AVAILABLE ITEMS BY CATEGORY                              *~-
-~*  Character: name, title,                                  *~-
-~*  virding, subclass, lineage, god,                         *~-
-~*  daler, xp_vis, xp_kap, xp_sei, xp_aud,                   *~-
-~*  gp_sei, gp_vig, gp_rad, fury                             *~-
-~*  Skills: gather, scavenge, farm                           *~-
-~*  City: city, buildings                                    *~-
-~*  Garrison: pool, stationed, gcap, raid                    *~-
-~*  Fleet: ships, dock, voyage                               *~-
-~*  Warehouse: stock, capacity, fish, grain, timber, iron,   *~-
-~*  furs, mead, amber, runes, spoils                         *~-
-~*  Missions: active, quota, refresh, errand                 *~-
-~*  Gods: patron, boons                                      *~-
-~*  Mushrooms: pouch, plots                                  *~-
-~*  Relics: relics, bonus                                    *~-
-~*  Reputation: midgard, lodbrok,                            *~-
-~*  eiriksson, uimair, rurikid,                              *~-
-~*  harfagre, yngling, skallagrim, stenkil, sverker,         *~-
-~*  eric, munso, skjoldung, sigurdsson,                      *~-
-~*  holmgard, eiriksby, imaird, hafrfjord, uppsala,          *~-
-~*  borgarfjord, vestergotland, sverkersby, ericsgard,       *~-
-~*  birka, lejre, nidaros                                    *~-
-~*  Weapon: weapon                                           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vdash list to see available items and your layout.    *~-
-~*  2) vdash add <item> to add specific data to display.     *~-
-~*  3) vdash remove <item> to remove unwanted items.         *~-
-~*  4) vdash order <item1>                                   *~-
-~*  <item2>... to reorder everything.                        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Unknown item: use vdash list to see valid item names.    *~-
-~*  Item already present: cannot add duplicates.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vdash                                                    *~-
-~*  vdash add daler                                          *~-
-~*  vdash add ships                                          *~-
-~*  vdash add birka                                          *~-
-~*  vdash remove gather                                      *~-
-~*  vdash order name daler ships birka quota                 *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vstats, vskills, vcity, vbuild, vrep           *~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Vdiscard                                                 *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  vdiscard - Warehouse Goods & Freshness Management        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  SYNTAX                                                   *~-
-~*  vdiscard     show warehouse stock and freshness          *~-
-~*  vdiscard stale  discard all fully expired goods          *~-
-~*  vdiscard stale <good>  discard expired lots for one good  *~-
-~*  vdiscard set  show auto-feed setting                     *~-
-~*  vdiscard set <level>  set auto-feed threshold            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vdiscard to inspect warehouse freshness at a glance.  *~-
-~*  2) Set auto-feed threshold with vdiscard set <level>.    *~-
-~*  3) Manually clear expired lots with vdiscard stale.      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  FRESHNESS                                                *~-
-~*  Perishable goods (grain, fish, mead, furs) degrade       *~-
-~*  over time.  Quality drops from fresh to slightly         *~-
-~*  stale, stale, old, and finally expires entirely.         *~-
-~*  Iron, timber, amber, and runestones never decay.         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  FRESHNESS COLOURS                                        *~-
-~*  fresh        shown in bright green                       *~-
-~*  slightly stale  shown in yellow                          *~-
-~*  stale        shown in brown                              *~-
-~*  old / expired   shown in red                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  AUTO-FEED (vdiscard set)                                 *~-
-~*  When auto-feed is enabled, goods that fall to or         *~-
-~*  below the chosen quality threshold are automatically     *~-
-~*  distributed to your townspeople instead of rotting.      *~-
-~*  This gives a small settler mood bonus.                   *~-
-~*  off           goods rot and are lost                     *~-
-~*  slightly stale  feed at 90% quality                      *~-
-~*  stale           feed at 78% quality                      *~-
-~*  old             feed at 62% quality                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  No effect from stale clear: no expired lots found.       *~-
-~*  Settler feed odd: verify current auto-feed               *~-
-~*  threshold with vdiscard set.                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  Example: vdiscard set stale                              *~-
-~*  Example: vdiscard stale fish                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vtrade, vbuild                                 *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Vdraw                                                    *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vdraw <weapon>                                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Draw a guild weapon you have forged at the Midgard       *~-
-~*  Smithy.  Use vdraw alone to refresh the currently        *~-
-~*  drawn weapon or clear a stale record.                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Types: breidox  langsverd  sverd  ox  stafr  spjot       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-

-~*  vdraw breidox                                            *~-
-~*  vdraw sverd                                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-

-~*  2) vdraw <type> to draw the weapon.                      *~-
-~*  3) vsheath when done to stow it.                         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Unknown type: check types list above.                    *~-

-~*  Vevents                                                  *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vevents                                           *~-
-~*  vevents <n>                                              *~-
-~*  vevents all                                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Shows recent events logged for your settlement:          *~-
-~*  boon grants, world events, raids, trade, voyages,        *~-
-~*  building completions, and more.                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  SUBCOMMANDS                                              *~-
-~*  vevents      show the last 10 events                     *~-
-~*  vevents <n>  show the last n events (max 50)             *~-
-~*  vevents all  show all stored events (up to 100)          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vevents to check recent settlement activity.          *~-
-~*  2) vevents all to review the full history.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-

-~*  settlement.  Events accumulate as things happen.         *~-

-~*  Vfarm                                                    *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vfarm                                             *~-
-~*  vfarm plant <mushroom> [slot]                            *~-
-~*  vfarm harvest [slot|all]                                 *~-
-~*  vfarm clear <slot>                                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Manage mushroom plots in your Farm.  Each Farm           *~-
-~*  tier adds 3 plot slots (T1=3, T2=6, and so on).          *~-
-~*  Requires the Farm building and the shroom quest.         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Plant a spore from your pouch.  Plots ripen over         *~-
-~*  2.5 to 3.5 real days.  You receive a message when        *~-
-~*  a plot is ready.  Harvesting auto-replants the           *~-
-~*  same spore type.  Use clear to uproot without            *~-
-~*  yield.                                                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Farming skill (0-200) improves harvest quality.          *~-
-~*  Higher skill increases the chance of harvesting          *~-
-~*  higher-tier mushrooms from your plots.                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vfarm plant <mushroom> [slot] to start a plot.        *~-
-~*  2) Wait for ready notification.                          *~-
-~*  3) vfarm harvest [slot|all] to collect yield.            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  No spores in pouch: restock from your mushroom route.    *~-
-~*  Invalid slot or occupied slot: check farm status first.  *~-
-~*  No ready crop: wait until the growth window completes.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vfarm plant cordyceps A1                                 *~-
-~*  vfarm harvest all                                        *~-
-~*  vfarm clear B2                                           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vcity, vbuild, vquest                          *~-

-~*  Vgod                                                     *~-

-~*  vgod tides                                               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Choose a patron god or view your current devotion.       *~-
-~*  Each god grants a set of unique spells.  Devotion        *~-
-~*  grows with use and unlocks deeper gifts.                 *~-
-~*  God entries also show brief omens that hint at each      *~-
-~*  deity's realm without fully revealing outcomes.          *~-
-~*  The display also shows which god is currently in power   *~-
-~*  and when the next god-turn will occur.                   *~-
-~*  Use vgod tides to inspect rite-driven favor pull for     *~-
-~*  the upcoming god-power rotation.                         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vgod to inspect current patron and standing.          *~-
-~*  2) vgod <name> then vgod <name> confirm to swear oath.   *~-
-~*  3) vgod tides to inspect current favor pull rankings.    *~-
-~*  4) Use vcast and vblot to deepen patron progression.     *~-

-~*  Vguard                                                   *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vguard                                            *~-
-~*  vguard recruit [name|#]                                  *~-
-~*  vguard enlist <name|#>                                   *~-
-~*  vguard muster | stand down                               *~-
-~*  vguard garrison <name|#|all>                             *~-
-~*  vguard recall <name|#|all>                               *~-
-~*  vguard war cry | shield wall                             *~-
-~*  vguard mode <name|#|all> <neutral|offensive|defensive>   *~-
-~*  vguard info|release|discharge <name|#>                   *~-
-~*  vguard bonds                                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Manage your personal named hirdmadrs.  Muster them       *~-
-~*  to join you in battle, or dismiss them to the pool.      *~-
-~*  Station guards on garrison duty to defend your city      *~-
-~*  and designate a champion.  Set each guard stance to      *~-
-~*  neutral, offensive, or defensive.                        *~-
-~*  Requires the Vegr Hersins path.                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  GARRISON & CHAMPION                                      *~-
-~*  Use vguard garrison to station named hirdmadrs on        *~-
-~*  city garrison duty.  The highest-level garrisoned        *~-
-~*  guard becomes the Garrison Champion and adds +3          *~-
-~*  defence power against incoming raids.                    *~-
-~*  Tiebreaker: most kills, then loyalty, then seniority.    *~-
-~*  Use vguard recall to return them to the city pool.       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  MUSTERED CHAMPION                                        *~-
-~*  When mustered, the highest-level personal guard          *~-
-~*  becomes the Mustered Champion.  All squad members        *~-
-~*  gain +1 atk and +1 def while the champion is present.    *~-
-~*  A guard can only hold one champion role at a time.       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vguard to inspect your active guard line.             *~-
-~*  2) vguard recruit / vguard enlist to add named guards.   *~-
-~*  3) vguard mode <name|#|all> <stance> to set behavior.    *~-
-~*  4) vguard garrison <name> to station city defenders.     *~-
-~*  5) vguard muster to call the rest to personal guard.     *~-
-~*  6) vguard stand down to return them to city_pool.        *~-
-~*  7) Wounded guards auto-remuster                          *~-
-~*  when recovery timer expires.                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  No available named guards in pool to muster.             *~-
-~*  Guard cap reached for current investment level.          *~-
-~*  Invalid mode. Use neutral, offensive, or defensive.      *~-
-~*  Cannot garrison a wounded or already-mustered guard.     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vguard                                                   *~-
-~*  vguard garrison all                                      *~-
-~*  vguard recall sigrid                                     *~-
-~*  vguard mode all defensive                                *~-
-~*  vguard mode sigrid offensive                             *~-
-~*  vguard bonds                                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vhird, vgarrison                               *~-

-~*  Vholm                                                    *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vholm challenge <player>                          *~-
-~*  vholm npc                                                *~-
-~*  vholm accept                                             *~-
-~*  vholm decline                                            *~-
-~*  vholm <off> <def>                                        *~-
-~*  vholm stats                                              *~-
-~*  vholm toplist                                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Participate in the holmgang ritual duel system.          *~-
-~*  Challenge another Viking or Styrmir the Unkillable       *~-
-~*  to a one-on-one duel on the holmgang ground.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  During a duel, submit your move each round with          *~-
-~*  vholm <offensive> <defensive>.  Both moves are           *~-
-~*  resolved simultaneously when both parties submit.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Duels are limited to once per 24 hours.  Leaving         *~-
-~*  the arena mid-duel forfeits the match.                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vholm challenge <player> or vholm npc.                *~-
-~*  2) Opponent uses vholm accept.                           *~-
-~*  3) Submit rounds with vholm <off> <def>.                 *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Cooldown active from recent duel.                        *~-
-~*  Opponent not eligible, absent, or not accepted yet.      *~-
-~*  Invalid move pair: check expected off/def options.       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vholm challenge skuggis                                  *~-
-~*  vholm accept                                             *~-
-~*  vholm cut parry                                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-

-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Invoke the leidangr: call forth sworn warriors           *~-
-~*  from all 13 lineage towns in three rapid waves,          *~-
-~*  each wave dealing guild-level-scaled melee damage        *~-
-~*  to your current target.                                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Requires the Ledung rally quest complete and at          *~-
-~*  least 1 charge available.  Only fires in combat.         *~-
-~*  Charges refill after 45 minutes.                         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Use vquest ledung to track per-town rally progress.      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Complete Ledung quest milestones first.               *~-
-~*  2) Enter combat and trigger vledung on a live target.    *~-
-~*  3) Track charge recovery between uses.                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  No fire when out of combat or with zero charges.         *~-

-~*  Vlongship                                                *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vlongship                                         *~-
-~*  vlongship build [name]                                   *~-
-~*  vlongship upgrade <name>                                 *~-
-~*  vlongship raid <village>                                 *~-
-~*  vlongship cancel <name>                                  *~-
-~*  vlongship rename <name> to <new>                         *~-
-~*  vlongship hold <name>                                    *~-
-~*  vlongship unhold <name>                                  *~-
-~*  vlongship targets                                        *~-
-~*  vlongship revenge                                        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Manage your longship fleet.  Ships can be sent on        *~-
-~*  raids, upgraded, renamed, and crewed with                *~-
-~*  hirdmadrs.  Use vlongship alone to see your              *~-
-~*  current fleet, timers, and crew readiness.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  hold marks a ship as held (shown with * prefix).         *~-
-~*  Held ships are skipped by "vlongship raid all".          *~-
-~*  Use unhold to remove the hold flag.                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  cancel recalls a ship from an active raid at full        *~-
-~*  penalty (no spoils, crew return with no XP).             *~-
-~*  targets lists valid raid destinations.  revenge          *~-
-~*  shows your current revenge window and any active         *~-
-~*  spoils bonus against the retaliating target.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vlongship build [name] to add a hull.                 *~-
-~*  2) vlongship upgrade <name> to improve capacity.         *~-
-~*  3) vlongship raid <village> or use vvoyage for           *~-
-~*  advanced contract sailing.                               *~-
-~*  4) vlongship cancel <name> to abort if needed.           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  No ship by that name: check vlongship output first.      *~-
-~*  Insufficient crew/readiness: assign hird and retry.      *~-
-~*  No valid target: use vlongship targets for current       *~-
-~*  raid destinations.                                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vlongship build Stormcrow                                *~-
-~*  vlongship upgrade Stormcrow                              *~-
-~*  vlongship hold Stormcrow                                 *~-
-~*  vlongship raid Austerfall                                *~-
-~*  vlongship cancel Stormcrow                               *~-
-~*  vlongship targets                                        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vhird, vraidcall                               *~-

-~*  Vmission                                                 *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vmission                                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  View and manage your active town missions.  Villages     *~-
-~*  offer tasks in exchange for daler and reputation.        *~-
-~*  Missions expire if not completed in time.                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Use vmission newbie for small fetch errands that pay     *~-
-~*  daler and goods without needing village reputation.      *~-
-~*  Use vmission repair to browse and settle hostile         *~-
-~*  standing debts through a separate repair-mission lane.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vmission to review available and active tasks.        *~-
-~*  2) Accept missions you can supply soon.                  *~-
-~*  3) Deliver goods/daler before expiry for rewards.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Mission expired before delivery: accept fresh offers.    *~-
-~*  Missing warehouse goods: buy, gather, or trade first.    *~-
-~*  Low daler for mission payment: top up funds first.       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-

-~*  Vmodrsokn                                                *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vmodrsokn [seid|vig|rad]                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Channel your fury inward, converting battle-rage         *~-
-~*  into guild point recovery.  Burns all current fury.      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  With no argument the yield splits across all three       *~-
-~*  pools.  Name a single pool to focus the conversion       *~-
-~*  there (75% efficiency, but all to one pool).             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Scales with guild level, wisdom, and seidgerd.           *~-
-~*  Higher fury = more GP.  Minimum 15 fury to use.          *~-
-~*  45s cooldown (reduced by berserksgangr).                 *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Build fury in combat.                                 *~-
-~*  2) Use vmodrsokn for split recovery or target one pool.  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vmodrsokn                                                *~-

-~*  Vmonument                                                *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vmonument                                         *~-
-~*  vmonument inscribe <feat title>                          *~-
-~*  vmonument remove <n>                                     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Manage runic monuments in your settlement.               *~-
-~*  Each monument carved from an earned feat adds            *~-
-~*  +2 settler mood permanently.                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Slot cap: guild_level / 5  (GL 20 = 4 slots).            *~-
-~*  Only feats you have earned can be inscribed.             *~-
-~*  Use vfeats to see eligible feats.                        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vfeats to choose eligible monument titles.            *~-
-~*  2) vmonument inscribe <feat title> to add one.           *~-
-~*  3) vmonument remove <n> to free a slot.                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Cannot inscribe titles you have not earned.              *~-
-~*  Slot cap reached: remove one before adding another.      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-

-~*  vmonument remove 2                                       *~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Vrecommend                                               *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vrecommend add <player>                           *~-
-~*  vrecommend remove <player>                               *~-
-~*  vrecommend list                                          *~-
-~*  vrecommend check <player>                                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Manage the guild recommendation list. Players must be    *~-
-~*  recommended by an admin (Kennari/Trainer or higher)      *~-
-~*  before they can enter Midgard or join the Vikings.       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  WHO CAN USE THIS                                         *~-
-~*  Kennari (VIKING_TRAINER) and higher rank only.           *~-
-~*  Viking Players and Initiates cannot use this command.    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  HOW IT WORKS                                             *~-
-~*  The gatekeeper Ulfr Ketilsson blocks all non-members     *~-
-~*  from entering Midgard unless they are on this list.      *~-
-~*  When a recommended player joins, they are automatically  *~-
-~*  removed from the list (one-time use).                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  NOTIFICATION                                             *~-
-~*  When added, online players receive a message:            *~-
-~*  "You have been recommended for                           *~-
-~*  entry into the Viking guild!"                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vrecommend add <player> to approve them               *~-
-~*  2) Player visits gatekeeper Ulfr at entrance             *~-
-~*  3) Player says "join vikings" and is admitted            *~-
-~*  4) Recommendation auto-removed on successful join        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Players must approach the gatekeeper themselves.         *~-
-~*  Recommendations do not expire until used or removed.     *~-
-~*  Only one recommendation per player at a time.            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vrecommend add newplayer                                 *~-
-~*  vrecommend check newplayer                               *~-
-~*  vrecommend list                                          *~-
-~*  vrecommend remove oldplayer                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vban, vguard                                   *~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vrecover                                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Recovers your guild object if it has been lost or        *~-
-~*  needs to be reloaded.  Use if things feel broken.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vrecover                                                 *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Run vrecover to inspect current state.                *~-
-~*  2) Apply the subcommand or option you need.              *~-
-~*  3) Re-run vrecover to verify results.                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-

-~*  Check syntax here and retry.                             *~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Vreflex                                                  *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vreflex                                           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  View and configure automatic combat reflexes.            *~-
-~*  Reflexes fire commands when a stat crosses a threshold.  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  SYNTAX                                                   *~-
-~*  vreflex - show configured reflexes                       *~-
-~*  vreflex add <stat> <threshold> [combat|always] <cmd>     *~-
-~*  vreflex remove <stat> <threshold> - remove a reflex      *~-
-~*  vreflex clear - remove all reflexes                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  STATS                                                    *~-
-~*  hp  fury  seid  vig  rad                                 *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  THRESHOLD FORMAT                                         *~-
-~*  Thresholds may be a percentage of                        *~-
-~*  max or an absolute value.                                *~-
-~*  Prefix with > to trigger when ABOVE,                     *~-
-~*  otherwise triggers at/below.                             *~-
-~*  50%   - fires at or below 50% of your max                *~-
-~*  250   - fires at or below 250 absolute                   *~-
-~*  >80%  - fires at or above 80% of your max                *~-
-~*  >500  - fires at or above 500 absolute                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  MODES                                                    *~-
-~*  combat (default) - only fires during combat.             *~-
-~*  always           - fires any time, even out of combat.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vreflex add hp 30% quaff healing                         *~-
-~*  vreflex add hp 30% combat quaff healing                  *~-
-~*  vreflex add fury >80% combat vberserk                    *~-
-~*  vreflex add vig 20% say Running low on Vig!              *~-
-~*  vreflex add seid >90% cast galdr                         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vskills                                        *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*  Vrelic                                                   *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vrelic                                            *~-
-~*  vrelic display <id> [n]                                  *~-
-~*  vrelic stow <id> [n]                                     *~-
-~*  vrelic adorn <n>                                         *~-
-~*  vrelic unadorn <n>                                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Manage the relics recovered from advanced voyages.       *~-
-~*  Displayed stat relics consume city slots and grant       *~-
-~*  live bonuses while active.  Cosmetic relics do not       *~-
-~*  use slots and are only decorative.                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  display      Place a stored stat relic in your city.     *~-
-~*  stow         Remove a displayed stat relic.              *~-
-~*  adorn        Place a cosmetic relic from storage.        *~-
-~*  unadorn      Remove a displayed cosmetic relic.          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vrelic                                                   *~-
-~*  vrelic display 102                                       *~-
-~*  vrelic stow 102                                          *~-

-~*  2) Apply the subcommand or option you need.              *~-
-~*  3) Re-run vrelic to verify results.                      *~-

-~*  Vrep                                                     *~-

-~*  Show your trade reputation                               *~-
-~*  rank at every Viking village.                            *~-
-~*  Displays reputation progress                             *~-
-~*  bars and rank names for all                              *~-

-~*  Gestur     = Guest                                       *~-
-~*  Kaupmadur  = Merchant                                    *~-
-~*  Vinur      = Friend                                      *~-
-~*  Arsmadur   = Trusted (maximum rank)                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-

-~*  Vscavenge                                                *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vscavenge                                         *~-
-~*  vscavenge <corpse>                                       *~-
-~*  vscavenge corpse 2                                       *~-
-~*  vscavenge orc corpse                                     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Strip battle spoils from a fallen enemy. Spoils are      *~-
-~*  stored in your city warehouse and consumed by your       *~-
-~*  settlers each tick to raise their dignity. Spoils        *~-
-~*  can also be sold to lineage villages via trade carts.    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Each corpse can only be scavenged once. Success chance   *~-
-~*  starts at 3% and rises to 10% cap as your scavenging     *~-
-~*  skill (0-200) grows. Skill is derived from lifetime      *~-
-~*  successful scavenges: 360                                *~-
-~*  scavenges per level (max 200).                           *~-
-~*  Higher enemy level increases success chance.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vscavenge                                                *~-
-~*  vscavenge orc corpse                                     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Kill an enemy.                                        *~-
-~*  2) Run vscavenge (or enable vtoggle auto_scavenge).      *~-
-~*  3) Check vtrade warehouse to see spoils balance.         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vtrade, vtoggle, vcity                         *~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Vsettler                                                 *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vsettler [status]                                 *~-
-~*  vsettler tax <level>                                     *~-
-~*  vsettler stock                                           *~-
-~*  vsettler housing                                         *~-
-~*  vsettler housing build                                   *~-
-~*  vsettler housing upgrade <1|2|3>                         *~-
-~*  vsettler community                                       *~-
-~*  vsettler community upgrade <building>                    *~-
-~*  vsettler edict [open_gates|workdrive|levy]               *~-
-~*  vsettler action <name>                                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Manage your settler community.  Settlers live in         *~-
-~*  Hearth Quarters, need food and                           *~-
-~*  water from your warehouse,                               *~-
-~*  and mead for morale.  Community buildings add jobs,      *~-
-~*  security, dignity, and production bonuses.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Settler mood (0-100) drives migration: happy settlers    *~-
-~*  attract newcomers; unhappy ones leave over time.         *~-
-~*  Mood is influenced by tax rate, housing quality, food,   *~-
-~*  water supply, active edicts, and governance scores.      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  GOVERNANCE                                               *~-
-~*  Security and Dignity each run 0-100 and modify           *~-
-~*  long-term settler retention and productivity.            *~-
-~*  Employment tracks how many settlers hold city jobs;      *~-
-~*  Flourishing is a combined milestone flag.                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  HOUSING (Hearth Quarters)                                *~-
-~*  housing      show all Hearth Quarter plots and totals    *~-
-~*  housing build  build a new Tier 1 Hearth Quarter         *~-
-~*  housing upgrade <N>  upgrade one T(N) plot to            *~-
-~*                       T(N+1), where N is 1-3              *~-
-~*  Housing construction takes time, like vbuild.            *~-
-~*  Completion is announced automatically.  Check            *~-
-~*  pending projects with vsettler status.                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMUNITY BUILDINGS                                      *~-
-~*  community    show all community buildings                *~-
-~*  community upgrade <bld>  upgrade that building one tier     *~-
-~*  Community buildings (market, workyard, watch, law,       *~-
-~*  poorhouse, midwife, timberward) provide jobs, security,  *~-
-~*  dignity, and production bonuses.  Each upgrade also      *~-
-~*  takes timed construction.                                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EDICTS (long policy, 6h duration, 18h cooldown)          *~-
-~*  edict        show current edict status and options       *~-
-~*  edict open_gates  Open Gates -- +15%                     *~-
-~*                    arrivals, costs 50 daler               *~-
-~*  edict workdrive  Work Drive -- production up, mood down  *~-
-~*  edict levy   Emergency Levy -- income spike, mood hit    *~-
-~*  One edict at a time; each has a cooldown after it ends.  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  ACTIONS (short civic actions with costs)                 *~-
-~*  action feast  mood surge, costs mead                     *~-
-~*                + grain + 300 daler                        *~-
-~*  action assembly  security and dignity                    *~-
-~*                   boost, costs 220 daler                  *~-
-~*  action watch  security boost, costs 250 daler            *~-
-~*  action crafts  production + mood boost, costs            *~-
-~*                 260 daler + materials                     *~-
-~*  action relief  dignity and mood                          *~-
-~*                 recovery, costs 450 daler                 *~-
-~*  action works  resilience and dignity boost, costs 350    *~-
-~*                daler + timber + iron                      *~-
-~*  One action at a time. Cooldown                           *~-
-~*  shows under vsettler status.                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  TAX LEVELS                                               *~-
-~*  tax none     no tax, best morale                         *~-
-~*  tax light    modest income, slight morale hit            *~-
-~*  tax moderate  balanced income and morale                 *~-
-~*  tax heavy    high income, morale penalty                 *~-
-~*  tax extortionate  maximum income, severe morale hit      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vsettler status to see population, mood, governance.  *~-
-~*  2) Build Hearth Quarters to raise population cap.        *~-
-~*  3) Upgrade community buildings                           *~-
-~*  to add jobs and security.                                *~-
-~*  4) Adjust tax and use edicts to fine-tune mood.          *~-
-~*  5) Keep food, water, and mead supply stable.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Population decline: check mood, food, and water supply.  *~-
-~*  Low security or dignity: upgrade community buildings.    *~-
-~*  Pending projects stall: verify                           *~-
-~*  resource warehouse levels.                               *~-
-~*  Edict greyed out: check remaining cooldown in status.    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vsettler status                                          *~-
-~*  vsettler housing build                                   *~-
-~*  vsettler housing upgrade 2                               *~-
-~*  vsettler community upgrade market                        *~-
-~*  vsettler edict open_gates                                *~-
-~*  vsettler action feast                                    *~-
-~*  vsettler tax moderate                                    *~-
-~*  vsettler stock                                           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vcity, vbuild                                  *~-
