-~*  Vspells                                                  *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vspells                                           *~-
-~*  vspells <god | category>                                 *~-
-~*  vspells autocast                                         *~-
-~*  vspells autocast add <spell>                             *~-
-~*  vspells autocast remove <spell>                          *~-
-~*  vspells autocast toggle <spell>                          *~-
-~*  vspells autocast prio <spell> <1-10>                     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Lists all galdrar (incantations) tied to your            *~-
-~*  patron god.  Filter by god name or category code:        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  d / vorn     Vorn -- defensive spells                    *~-
-~*  o / nid      Nid -- offensive spells                     *~-
-~*  e / tof      Tofrar -- enchantments                      *~-
-~*  h / bot      Bot -- healing spells                       *~-
-~*  v / spa      Spa -- divination spells                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  AUTOCAST MANAGEMENT                                      *~-
-~*  autocast     show autocast list and slot usage           *~-
-~*  autocast add <spell>  add spell to autocast              *~-
-~*                        (starts enabled)                   *~-
-~*  autocast remove <spell>  remove spell from                  *~-
-~*                        autocast entirely                  *~-
-~*  autocast toggle <spell>  pause or resume a                  *~-
-~*                        spell in the list                  *~-
-~*  autocast prio <s> <n>  set cast priority 1                *~-
-~*                        (low) to 10 (high)                 *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vspells to view your current spell table.             *~-
-~*  2) Filter by god/category to plan loadout.               *~-
-~*  3) vspells autocast add <spell> to queue a spell.        *~-
-~*  4) Use toggle to pause it without removing it.           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Unknown spell/category alias: use listed codes.          *~-
-~*  Slot cap reached: check slot usage in autocast view.     *~-
-~*  Toggle on spell not in list: use add first.              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-

-~*  vspells autocast remove stormkall                        *~-

-~*  with Orm the Brawler in Midgard.                         *~-

-~*  Vswitch                                                  *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vswitch <target>                                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Redirect your attacks to a different enemy in the        *~-
-~*  room while staying in combat.  Your prior target         *~-
-~*  continues attacking you; only your output shifts.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  You must already be in combat.  The new target           *~-
-~*  must be present in the same room.                        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Not currently in combat with an eligible target.         *~-
-~*  Named target absent or invalid for switch.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vswitch troll                                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Run vswitch to inspect current state.                 *~-
-~*  2) Apply the subcommand or option you need.              *~-
-~*  3) Re-run vswitch to verify results.                     *~-

-~*  Vtattoo                                                  *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vtattoo                                           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  View and apply tattoos to your character.  Tattoos       *~-
-~*  are permanent marks of identity and achievement.         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  INSCRIPTION                                              *~-
-~*  Vikings can inscribe rune tattoos on others.             *~-
-~*  Syntax: vtattoo inscribe <player> <pattern> <slot>       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  PATTERNS                                                 *~-
-~*  Aegishjalmur (Helm of Awe)    - protection               *~-
-~*  Valknut (Warrior Knot)        - battle prowess           *~-
-~*  Yggdrasil (World Tree)        - life and vigor           *~-
-~*  Jormungandr (World Serpent)   - elemental warding        *~-
-~*  Hamr (Wild Shape)             - battle fury              *~-
-~*  Thruma (Thunder's Voice)       - storm's answer          *~-
-~*  Styrkr (Raw Might)            - strength of sinew        *~-
-~*  Vindr (Wind-Swift)            - fleetness of limb        *~-
-~*  Thol (Enduring Flesh)         - patience of stone        *~-
-~*  Skilningr (Hidden Lore)       - whispered wisdom         *~-
-~*  Viss (Second Sight)           - the deeper knowing       *~-
-~*  Ordljomr (Silver Tongue)      - skald's gift             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  SLOTS                                                    *~-
-~*  body  chest  legs  head  hands                           *~-
-~*  back  feet   neck  finger                                *~-
-~*  knees  elbows (half effect)                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  RITUAL                                                   *~-
-~*  Inscription takes 2 minutes to complete.                 *~-
-~*  The target must accept; both are held still.             *~-
-~*  Cooldown: 24 hours per inscriber.                        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vtattoo to view your own marks.                       *~-
-~*  2) vtattoo inscribe to offer a rune tattoo.              *~-
-~*  3) Target uses accept inscription to receive.            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-

-~*  Vthing                                                   *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vthing                                            *~-
-~*  vthing vote <target>                                     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  The Thing is the weekly assembly that names the          *~-
-~*  raid target.  A new target is chosen each Monday         *~-
-~*  at midnight UTC from the top-voted option.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  vthing alone shows the current target, time              *~-
-~*  remaining, and the live vote tally.                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Cast your vote with vthing vote <target>.                *~-
-~*  One vote per Viking per week.                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vthing to inspect current vote board and timer.       *~-
-~*  2) vthing vote <target> to cast your weekly vote.        *~-
-~*  3) Recheck vthing for tally changes through the week.    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-

-~*  Vthrall                                                  *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vthrall                                           *~-
-~*  vthrall assign <n> to <building>                         *~-
-~*  vthrall unassign <building>                              *~-
-~*  vthrall unassign all                                     *~-
-~*  vthrall claim [name]                                     *~-
-~*  vthrall release                                          *~-
-~*  vthrall name <name>                                      *~-
-~*  vthrall status                                           *~-
-~*  vthrall stay | follow | summon | dismiss                 *~-
-~*  vthrall give/get/drop <item|all>                         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Assign thralls from your Thrall Pen to buildings         *~-
-~*  for passive production bonuses each tick.                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Longhouse    +1 hirdmadr per thrall per tick             *~-
-~*  Warehouse    +2 days max age per thrall (slower rot)     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  You may also claim one thrall as a personal              *~-
-~*  companion.  A claimed follower can carry items,          *~-
-~*  be ordered to stay or follow, and gains combat XP        *~-
-~*  while fighting in the same room as you.                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Thralls remain in the pen and count toward cap.          *~-
-~*  Max assignment: pen_cap / 2 per building.                *~-
-~*  Assignments and follower progress persist.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Thralls have a 5% chance per tick to die (all tiers).    *~-
-~*  T1 Thrall Pen has escape risk; T2+ pens do not.          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vthrall status to review pen capacity and usage.      *~-
-~*  2) vthrall assign <n> to <building> for bonuses.         *~-
-~*  3) Optionally claim one thrall as companion.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  No Thrall Pen or low tier: build or upgrade first.       *~-
-~*  Assignment exceeds building cap: lower amount or expand  *~-
-~*  pen/building capacity.                                   *~-
-~*  Companion commands fail when no thrall is currently      *~-
-~*  claimed.                                                 *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vthrall status                                           *~-
-~*  vthrall assign 6 to longhouse                            *~-
-~*  vthrall claim Einar                                      *~-
-~*  vthrall follow                                           *~-
-~*  vthrall release                                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vcity, vbuild, vhird, vgarrison                *~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Vthrek                                                   *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vthrek                                            *~-
-~*  vthrek trigger <1-99>                                    *~-
-~*  vthrek absorb  <1-90>                                    *~-
-~*  vthrek bleed   <1-75>                                    *~-
-~*  vthrek reset                                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Configure your Threk endurance pool.  Large hits         *~-
-~*  that reach the trigger threshold are partly soaked       *~-
-~*  into the pool instead of landing immediately.            *~-
-~*  The pool then bleeds back as HP damage each beat.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  trigger      Hit threshold as % of your max HP.          *~-
-~*  absorb       % of each qualifying hit that is soaked.    *~-
-~*  bleed        % of pool returned as damage per beat.      *~-
-~*  reset        Restore all three settings to defaults.     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  A hit qualifies if it meets trigger% of max HP           *~-
-~*  OR is >= 60 damage, whichever threshold is lower.        *~-
-~*  Pool cap: 150% max HP.  Absorption hard cap: 90%.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vthrek to review your current settings.               *~-
-~*  2) Tune trigger/absorb/bleed for your build.             *~-
-~*  3) Re-test in combat and adjust over time.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Unexpected spikes usually mean trigger set too high.     *~-
-~*  Too much bleed-back indicates bleed value is too high.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vthrek                                                   *~-
-~*  vthrek trigger 35                                        *~-
-~*  vthrek absorb 55                                         *~-
-~*  vthrek bleed 18                                          *~-
-~*  vthrek reset                                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vstats                                         *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*  Vtoggle                                                  *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vtoggle [name]                                    *~-
-~*  vtoggle god <name>                                       *~-
-~*  vtoggle god off                                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  View or flip optional automated behaviours.              *~-
-~*  All changes save immediately.                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  dest_corpse  Auto-destruct corpse after vrite.           *~-
-~*  auto_gather  Run vgather immediately after vrite.        *~-
-~*  auto_scavenge  Run vscavenge after each kill.            *~-
-~*  auto_charge  Fire vcharge at start of each fight.        *~-
-~*  auto_bloodeagle  Fire vbloodeagle at low enemy HP.       *~-
-~*  auto_warcry  Fire war cry whenever it is ready.          *~-
-~*  auto_shieldwall  Fire shield wall whenever ready.        *~-
-~*  hide_location  Hide your room name in vikings2.          *~-
-~*  hide_gps     Hide your entire row in vikings2.           *~-
-~*  numbers      Show damage totals in combat text.          *~-
-~*  brief_combat  Suppress chain/body-strike messages.       *~-
-~*  brief_spells  Suppress spell cast/effect messages.       *~-
-~*  brief_hird   Suppress hird guard combat messages.        *~-
-~*  brief_ward   Suppress ward absorb messages.              *~-
-~*  valhr_coffin  Valhr upkeep draws from carried coffin.    *~-
-~*  mip_voyage   Send voyage status updates over MIP.        *~-
-~*  rite_god     Set vrite devotion target god.              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Use vtoggle god <name> to direct vrite devotion to       *~-
-~*  a specific god, or vtoggle god off to revert to          *~-
-~*  your patron.                                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vtoggle to list current toggle state.                 *~-
-~*  2) Flip desired behavior flags one at a time.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck output to confirm saved state.                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Unknown toggle name: use vtoggle list output spelling.   *~-
-~*  Unexpected behavior often comes from old toggle state.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vtoggle                                                  *~-
-~*  vtoggle brief_spells                                     *~-
-~*  vtoggle hide_location                                    *~-
-~*  vtoggle god tyr                                          *~-
-~*  vtoggle god off                                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vikings2, hp, vsethp, vvoyage, vrite           *~-

-~*  Vtrade                                                   *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vtrade                                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Buy and sell goods with villages in the biome.           *~-
-~*  Each village wants different goods; prices shift         *~-
-~*  with supply.  Use vtrade alone to see options.           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  SYNTAX                                                   *~-
-~*  vtrade       show all trade options                      *~-
-~*  vtrade prices  current market prices                     *~-
-~*                 and next shift timer                      *~-
-~*  vtrade info  buy/sell prices at your current location    *~-
-~*  vtrade stock  warehouse stock contents and freshness     *~-
-~*  vtrade carts  all carts (dispatched                      *~-
-~*                and idle) with status                      *~-
-~*  vtrade dispatch  send a cart to buy or sell goods        *~-
-~*  vtrade market  player buy orders and fill orders         *~-
-~*  vtrade goods  settlement and good price overview         *~-
-~*  vtrade history  recent price history for a good          *~-
-~*  vtrade history all  price history summary for all goods  *~-
-~*  vtrade cap   set maximum stock amount for a good         *~-
-~*  vtrade block  reserve goods from being sold              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  CART MANAGEMENT                                          *~-
-~*  vtrade carts reinforce  overview of all carts              *~-
-~*                        with upgrade costs                 *~-
-~*  vtrade carts reinforce <id>  preview/confirm cart tier upgrade  *~-
-~*  vtrade carts repair <id>  preview/confirm cart               *~-
-~*                        durability repair                  *~-
-~*  vtrade carts rebuild <id>  preview/confirm                    *~-
-~*                        destroyed cart rebuild             *~-
-~*  vtrade carts recall <id>  recall dispatched                  *~-
-~*                        cart (15% penalty)                 *~-
-~*  Without <id>, reinforce shows                            *~-
-~*  upgrade costs for all carts.                             *~-
-~*  Without <id>, repair/rebuild shows                       *~-
-~*  same view as vtrade carts.                               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  DISPATCH SYNTAX                                          *~-
-~*  vtrade dispatch sell <amount> <good> <village>           *~-
-~*  vtrade dispatch buy  <amount> <good> <village>           *~-
-~*  [quality] [escort]                                       *~-
-~*  Perishable quality: fresh, oldest, stale, normal         *~-
-~*  Mead quality: green, young, maturing, well-aged, aged    *~-
-~*  Default: fresh (perishables), best mead (aged first)     *~-
-~*  Add escort after village to assign hirdmadrs.            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  MARKET SYNTAX                                            *~-
-~*  vtrade market post <amount>                              *~-
-~*  <good> <price> - post buy order                          *~-
-~*  vtrade market sell <amount> <good>                       *~-
-~*  <price> - post sell order                                *~-
-~*  vtrade market fill <order_id> [amount] - fill an order   *~-
-~*  vtrade market cancel <order_id> - cancel your order      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vtrade prices to see current market state.            *~-
-~*  2) vtrade stock to check warehouse contents.             *~-
-~*  3) vtrade dispatch buy|sell to send carts.               *~-
-~*  4) vtrade carts to collect returns and check status.     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Insufficient daler for buys:                             *~-
-~*  reduce quantity or earn more.                            *~-
-~*  Insufficient warehouse goods for sells: restock first.   *~-
-~*  No Trading Post: build one with                          *~-
-~*  vbuild start trading_post.                               *~-
-~*  No Warehouse: build one to sell goods                    *~-
-~*  (vbuild start warehouse).                                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vtrade                                                   *~-
-~*  vtrade prices                                            *~-
-~*  vtrade stock                                             *~-
-~*  vtrade dispatch buy 40 timber midgard                    *~-
-~*  vtrade dispatch sell 60 fish midgard                     *~-
-~*  vtrade dispatch sell 20 fish midgard fresh               *~-
-~*  vtrade dispatch sell 40 mead uppsala aged                *~-
-~*  vtrade dispatch sell 50 grain eiriksby fresh escort 2    *~-
-~*  vtrade goods                                             *~-
-~*  vtrade goods timber                                      *~-
-~*  vtrade history fish                                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vgather, vcity, vdiscard                       *~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Vtrain                                                   *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vtrain `<skill>                                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Train a skill using accumulated saga points.  Check      *~-
-~*  vskills to see what is available and vhelp skills        *~-
-~*  for cost details.  Training is permanent.                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Insufficient saga points or unmet prerequisites.         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vtrain berserksgangr                                     *~-
-~*  vskills                                                  *~-
-~*  vhelp skills berserksgangr                               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Run vtrain to inspect current state.                  *~-
-~*  2) Apply the subcommand or option you need.              *~-
-~*  3) Re-run vtrain to verify results.                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vskills                                        *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Vvalhr                                                   *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vvalhr                                            *~-
-~*  vvalhr status                                            *~-
-~*  vvalhr stop                                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Release the Valhrim -- the cold of the freshly-          *~-
-~*  slain -- across your party's enemies.  Enemies in        *~-
-~*  the room are marked; each combat heartbeat each          *~-
-~*  marked enemy has a chance to lose 1 AC as the            *~-
-~*  rime works into their joints.                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Requires 1 corpse in the room and at least one           *~-
-~*  other live party member present.                         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Every 10 combat rounds the tier advances and costs       *~-
-~*  that many more corpses as upkeep.  Missing upkeep        *~-
-~*  collapses the rime.  Use stop to end it manually.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  AC proc chance: 5% at tier 1, +3% per tier.              *~-
-~*  Toggle valhr_coffin draws upkeep from a carried          *~-
-~*  coffin instead of room corpses.                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Ensure party and corpse prerequisites are met.        *~-
-~*  2) vvalhr to begin rime effect in combat.                *~-
-~*  3) Check vvalhr status and stop when needed.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Missing corpse or no live party member present.          *~-
-~*  Upkeep collapses if corpse supply cannot sustain tiers.  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vvalhr                                                   *~-
-~*  vvalhr status                                            *~-
-~*  vvalhr stop                                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vtoggle                                        *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Vvarangian                                               *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vvarangian                                        *~-
-~*  vvarangian send <player> <n>                             *~-
-~*  vvarangian recall <player>                               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Dispatch hirdmadrs as Varangian Guards to another        *~-
-~*  Viking's city for up to 24 hours.  The receiver          *~-
-~*  gains temporary garrison defenders; you earn             *~-
-~*  2 daler per guard per trade tick (~3 hours).             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Guards leave your pool immediately on dispatch.          *~-
-~*  Max 20 per contract.  One active contract per            *~-
-~*  target at a time.  Use recall to cancel early.           *~-
-~*  Requires guild level 5.                                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Check available hird pool and target city need.       *~-
-~*  2) vvarangian send <player> <n> to dispatch guards.      *~-
-~*  3) vvarangian recall <player> to end early.              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Cannot send above cap or without sufficient pool size.   *~-
-~*  Only one active contract per target is allowed.          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vvarangian send skuggis 12                               *~-
-~*  vvarangian recall skuggis                                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vhird, vgarrison                               *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Vvoyage                                                  *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vvoyage                                           *~-
-~*  vvoyage launch <ship> [1-3]                              *~-
-~*  vvoyage chart                                            *~-
-~*  vvoyage queue <coord> [coord..]                          *~-
-~*  vvoyage hold | clear                                     *~-
-~*  vvoyage resolve <choice>                                 *~-
-~*  vvoyage continue                                         *~-
-~*  vvoyage end | abandon                                    *~-
-~*  vvoyage log                                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Send a real longship on a timed open-sea voyage.         *~-
-~*  Launching offers advanced contracts with different       *~-
-~*  risk profiles.  Once at sea you reveal chart tiles,      *~-
-~*  queue movement, resolve nodes, and bring home any        *~-
-~*  secured spoils when you dock.                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  BEFORE YOU LAUNCH                                        *~-
-~*  You need a built longship and enough crew benches        *~-
-~*  to safely handle the selected contract danger.           *~-
-~*  Only one active voyage can run at a time.                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  launch       Show or accept voyage                       *~-
-~*               contracts for a ship.                       *~-
-~*  chart        View the revealed sea chart.                *~-
-~*  queue        Queue one or more movement targets.         *~-
-~*  resolve      Choose how to handle a paused node.         *~-
-~*  continue     Skip a paused node and keep sailing.        *~-
-~*  end          Dock at a harbor and return with spoils.    *~-
-~*  abandon      End the voyage and dock the ship.           *~-
-~*  log          Show recent voyage events.                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vvoyage launch <ship> to view contracts.              *~-
-~*  2) vvoyage launch <ship> <1-3> to accept one.            *~-
-~*  3) vvoyage chart and vvoyage queue <coord..> to sail.    *~-
-~*  4) vvoyage resolve <choice> when paused nodes appear.    *~-
-~*  5) vvoyage end at harbor to secure spoils.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  No pending contracts for that ship: run launch first.    *~-
-~*  No active voyage for queue/resolve/end. Launch contract  *~-
-~*  first, then issue sea commands.                          *~-
-~*  Low ship tier or crew for the route. Choose a safer      *~-
-~*  contract, or upgrade hull and benches in vlongship.      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vvoyage launch Balle                                     *~-
-~*  vvoyage launch Balle 2                                   *~-
-~*  vvoyage queue C7 C8 D8                                   *~-
-~*  vvoyage resolve board                                    *~-
-~*  vvoyage end                                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Enable the mip_voyage toggle if you want voyage          *~-
-~*  status, chart, and log updates                           *~-
-~*  in a MIP-capable client UI.                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vlongship, vrelic, vtoggle                     *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Vweapons                                                 *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Usage: vweapons                                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Shows all guild weapons forged on your object.           *~-
-~*  Displays tier, proficiency level and bar, voyage         *~-
-~*  rune lore, and active elemental tempers.                 *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Types: breidox  langsverd  sverd  ox  stafr  spjot       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) vweapons to see forged weapons and their status.      *~-
-~*  2) vdraw <type> to draw a weapon.                        *~-
-~*  3) vsheath to stow it when done.                         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vweapons                                                 *~-
-~*  vdraw breidox                                            *~-
-~*  vsheath                                                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Nothing shown: no weapons forged yet.                    *~-
-~*  Visit Bjorn at the Midgard Smithy to forge one.          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vdraw, vsheath                                 *~-

-~*  Abilities                                                *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Abilities -- How They Are Unlocked                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  What abilities exist, and how each is unlocked.          *~-
-~*  Skill training specifics are in                          *~-
-~*  vskills and vhelp skills.                                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  AVAILABLE FROM JOIN                                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Combat                                                   *~-
-~*  vdraw / vsheath  Draw or sheath a weapon.                *~-
-~*  vcharge      Opening charge strike.  Not in combat.      *~-
-~*  vthrek       Configure the endurance                     *~-
-~*               pool (damage soak).                         *~-
-~*  vvalhr       Slaughter-rime:                             *~-
-~*               party/corpse combat effect.                 *~-
-~*  vreflex      Auto-fire commands from                     *~-
-~*               HP or fury triggers.                        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Devotion                                                 *~-
-~*  vblot        Sacrifice to your patron god.               *~-
-~*  vgod         View your deity's favour and offerings.     *~-
-~*  vcast        Cast spells. Spells                         *~-
-~*               unlock through devotion.                    *~-
-~*  vrite        Corpse rite -- restore guild points.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  City and Economy                                         *~-
-~*  vcity        Found and manage your settlement.           *~-
-~*  vbuild       Construct and upgrade buildings.            *~-
-~*  vfarm        Manage farmland and crop output.            *~-
-~*  vgather      Gather raw materials from the land.         *~-
-~*  vtrade       Send trade carts between cities.            *~-
-~*  vmission     Accept trade deliveries for daler.          *~-
-~*  vlongship    Build ships and launch raids.               *~-
-~*  vthrall      Direct thrall workers.                      *~-
-~*  vsettler     Manage city settlers.                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Social                                                   *~-
-~*  vthing       Vote on the weekly raid target.             *~-
-~*  vhird        Manage hird pool, garrison,                 *~-
-~*               and ship assignments.                       *~-
-~*  vguard       Muster named hirdmadrs as                   *~-
-~*               your personal guard.                        *~-
-~*  vholm        Challenge to or answer a holmgang duel.     *~-
-~*  vavenge      Track enemies marked for vengeance.         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Tracking                                                 *~-
-~*  vstats       Stats, resources, and combat readiness.     *~-
-~*  vscore       Detailed character score sheet.             *~-
-~*  vfeats       Iron-deeds and earned bynames.              *~-
-~*  vquest       Current quest progress.                     *~-
-~*  vmap         The biome map.                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  UNLOCKED BY GUILD LEVEL                                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  vvarangian   Guild level 5.   Hire out hirdmadrs.        *~-
-~*  vmodrsokn    Guild level 30.  Channel fury into GP.      *~-
-~*  shield wall  Lvl 45. Hirdmadrs close ranks around you.   *~-
-~*  vbloodeagle  Guild level 60.  Execute a wounded enemy.   *~-
-~*  war cry      Lvl 75. Hirdmadrs surge with battle fury.   *~-
-~*  vmonument    Guild level 90.  Raise runic monuments.     *~-
-~*  vberserk     Guild level 105. Enter berserk rage.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  UNLOCKED BY QUEST                                        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  vstrike -- Body strikes.  Start with a quest.            *~-
-~*  Orm the Brawler in Midgard can show you the way.         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  vtattoo -- Tattoos.  Requires the First Mark quest.      *~-
-~*  After that, patterns unlock via lineage standing.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  ENHANCED BY SKILLS                                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Some abilities deepen with skill investment.  No         *~-
-~*  skill is required to use them -- the right path          *~-
-~*  investment simply extends what each one can do.          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Armour mastery                                           *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Armour Mastery System                                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Armour mastery is a passive long-term progression        *~-
-~*  system.  You grow proficient in each armour slot         *~-
-~*  by taking hits while wearing it.                         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Slots: Helmet, Armour, Breastplate, Greaves,             *~-
-~*  Gloves, Boots, Cloak, Shield.                            *~-
-~*  Each slot has its own level and progress pool.           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  HOW IT WORKS                                             *~-
-~*  Every qualifying hit absorbed while wearing a slot       *~-
-~*  adds rounds to that slot's pool.  When the pool          *~-
-~*  crosses the next threshold the level increases.          *~-
-~*  All slot levels cap at 50.                               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMBAT EFFECT                                            *~-
-~*  Mastery amplifies the AC absorption your worn            *~-
-~*  armour already provided on that hit.  At level 50        *~-
-~*  across all 8 slots it can double effective AC.           *~-
-~*  Does not apply to thru-armour hits or when the           *~-
-~*  armour absorbed nothing from the hit.                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Use varmour to view current per-slot progress.           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-

-~*  Berserkja                                                *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Vegr Berserkja -- Path of the Berserker                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  The path of rage and relentless aggression.  Berser-     *~-
-~*  kers build fury as they fight, growing stronger with     *~-
-~*  each blow.  Deep investment makes the frenzy both        *~-
-~*  sustainable and devastating.                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Berserksgangr  Root skill.  Unlocks the path.            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  SECONDARY                                                *~-
-~*  Skills that extend and deepen the berserk state or       *~-
-~*  improve your overall combat capability.                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  TERTIARY                                                 *~-
-~*  Advanced options for those fully committed to rage.      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Use vhelp skills <skill> to learn what a skill does.     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-

-~*  Blot calendar                                            *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Blot Calendar -- Seasonal Bonuses                        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Five real-world date windows grant guild-wide            *~-
-~*  production and economic bonuses to all Vikings.          *~-
-~*  Bonuses are passive -- no action required.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Disablot                                                 *~-
-~*  Feb 1-14: +10% hirdmadr production per                   *~-
-~*  Longhouse tick.                                          *~-
-~*  Sigrblot                                                 *~-
-~*  Apr 9-22: +8% raid cargo when ships return.              *~-
-~*  Midsummarblot                                            *~-
-~*  Jun 20-Jul 3: +15% warehouse goods production.           *~-
-~*  Hokunblot    Oct 14-28:  -20% named hirdmadr upkeep.     *~-
-~*  Jolablot     Dec 21-Jan 3:  +1 settler mood per tick.    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  All dates are real-world calendar dates (UTC).           *~-
-~*  The active blot (if any) is shown in vstats              *~-
-~*  and at the top of the vwiz status page.                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-

-~*  Economy                                                  *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  The Viking Economy                                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  The guild economy revolves around daler (fame),          *~-
-~*  trade goods, and village reputation.                     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Daler        Fame currency.  Earned through deeds.       *~-
-~*  Trade        Buy/sell goods with biome villages.         *~-
-~*  Missions     Village tasks for daler and rep rewards.    *~-
-~*  Buildings    Unlock production and trade options.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Village reputation affects prices and what missions      *~-
-~*  are offered.  Build rep through consistent trade         *~-
-~*  and completing their requests.                           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-

-~*  If behavior differs, verify stats, toggles, resources.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vhelp general/economy                                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vtrade, vcity, vmission, vbuild                *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Farming                                                  *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Farming -- Field Skill                                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  The art of cultivating crops for food and trade.         *~-
-~*  Higher skill increases yield and crop quality.           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Farming is a field skill used in the Viking biome        *~-
-~*  to grow crops in your settlement fields. Use vfarm       *~-
-~*  to manage your crops and harvest them when ready.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Acquire seeds through trade or gathering.             *~-
-~*  2) Plant in your settlement fields with vfarm.           *~-
-~*  3) Harvest when mature for goods or trade.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vfarm, vskills, vtrade                         *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Feats                                                    *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Feats -- Permanent Marks of Achievement                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Feats are permanent records of what you have done        *~-
-~*  in the guild.  They are earned automatically as          *~-
-~*  you play; nothing needs to be activated.                 *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  HOW TO EARN FEATS                                        *~-
-~*  Feats are awarded for crossing milestones in your        *~-
-~*  guild history.  Categories include:                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Combat       Kill counts against enemies of all kinds.   *~-
-~*  Raids        Longship raids sent and completed.          *~-
-~*  Seid         Spells cast and spell damage dealt.         *~-
-~*  Rites        Corpse rites performed over time.           *~-
-~*  Buildings    Structures built in your city.              *~-
-~*  Trading      Goods traded and daler earned.              *~-
-~*  Devotion     Deepening your bond with a patron god.      *~-
-~*  Tenacity     Deaths survived and duels fought.           *~-
-~*  Crafting     Weapons forged and proficiency earned.      *~-
-~*  Guild Age    Time spent as a Viking.                     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  TYPES OF FEAT                                            *~-
-~*  Some feats are deeds -- markers of what you did.         *~-
-~*  Others are bynames -- titles others may see when         *~-
-~*  they look at you or read your score.                     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  FEAT WEIGHT                                              *~-
-~*  Every feat carries a weight reflecting its               *~-
-~*  difficulty: Drengr, Thegn, Hersir, Jarl, Fylkir.         *~-
-~*  Heavier feats mark rarer accomplishments.                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read this topic top-to-bottom once.                   *~-
-~*  2) Apply the related commands in small steps.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck this topic as your setup evolves.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Most issues come from skipped prerequisites.             *~-
-~*  If behavior differs, verify stats, toggles, resources.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vhelp general/feats                                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vfeats, vscore                                 *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Gathering                                                *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Gathering -- Field Skill                                 *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  The art of collecting raw materials from the wild.       *~-
-~*  Higher skill improves yield and                          *~-
-~*  variety of what you find.                                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Gathering works in the Viking                            *~-
-~*  biome or on slain enemies.                               *~-
-~*  Use vgather on a corpse to harvest materials from        *~-
-~*  your kill, or use it in the biome to find resources.     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Kill an enemy or travel to the Viking biome.          *~-
-~*  2) Use vgather on a corpse or in the biome.              *~-
-~*  3) Gather materials for trade or crafting.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vgather, vskills, vtrade                       *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Getting started                                          *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Getting Started                                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Step 1       Choose your lineage (vlineage).             *~-
-~*  Links you to a Norse bloodline and village.              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Step 2       Choose your patron god (vgod).              *~-
-~*  Grants spells and shapes your devotion.                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Step 3       Visit Midgard smithy and forge a weapon.    *~-
-~*  Types: breidox langsverd sverd ox stafr spjot.           *~-
-~*  Say 'forge <type>' to Bjorn Ironhand.                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Step 4       Set your first spells for autocast.         *~-
-~*  Use vcast/vspells and enable a simple auto setup.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Step 5       Learn your first skill (vtrain).            *~-
-~*  Check vskills to see what is available.                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Step 6       Run newbie missions                         *~-
-~*               first (vmission newbie).                    *~-
-~*  Build early daler and goods safely.                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Step 7       Then run regular missions (vmission).       *~-
-~*  Build village rep to unlock stronger options.            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Step 8       Recruit your first named hird               *~-
-~*               guard (vguard recruit).                     *~-
-~*  Guards add combat support and start your hird GXP flow.  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Step 9       Build a city when ready (vcity, vbuild).    *~-
-~*  Gives you a home base for trade and raids.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Step 10      Explore the biome (vmap).                   *~-
-~*  Trade, gather, and meet the villages.                    *~-
-~*  Need road carts?  See vhelp general/road_travel.         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Warband command note: vhelp hird explains how recruits   *~-
-~*  flow between vhird, personal guard (vguard), garrison,   *~-
-~*  and longship crews.                                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Take your time.  Discovery is part of the saga.          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read this topic top-to-bottom once.                   *~-
-~*  2) Apply the related commands in small steps.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck this topic as your setup evolves.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Most issues come from skipped prerequisites.             *~-
-~*  If behavior differs, verify stats, toggles, resources.   *~-

-~*  Hersins                                                  *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Vegr Hersins -- Path of the Jarl                         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  The path of command and leadership.  Jarls lead named    *~-
-~*  warriors into battle and grow their warband over time.   *~-
-~*  Investment improves guard strength and warband size.     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Root skill unlocks the path.                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  SECONDARY                                                *~-
-~*  Skills that improve guard strength and numbers.          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  TERTIARY                                                 *~-
-~*  Advanced tactics for seasoned warband commanders.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Use vhelp skills <skill> to learn what a skill does.     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read this topic top-to-bottom once.                   *~-
-~*  2) Apply the related commands in small steps.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck this topic as your setup evolves.             *~-

-~*  Most issues come from skipped prerequisites.             *~-
-~*  If behavior differs, verify stats, toggles, resources.   *~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Holmgang                                                 *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  The Holmgang -- Ritual Duel System                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  The holmgang is a formalised one-on-one combat rite.     *~-
-~*  Both parties step onto the hazel-marked ground and       *~-
-~*  submit moves simultaneously each round.  The duel        *~-
-~*  ends when one fighter is brought to zero.                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  LOCATION                                                 *~-
-~*  The holmgang ground is in the Viking guildhall.          *~-
-~*  Both challenger and target must be present to fight.     *~-
-~*  Stepping off the ground forfeits the duel.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  MOVES                                                    *~-
-~*  Each round you submit one offensive and one defensive    *~-
-~*  move: vholm <off> <def>.  Moves resolve together.        *~-
-~*  Offensive: slash thrust overhead feint                   *~-
-~*  Defensive: parry dodge block counter                     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COOLDOWN                                                 *~-
-~*  Each participant may only fight once per 24 hours.       *~-
-~*  Forfeiting by stepping off the ground still counts.      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  NPC PRACTICE                                             *~-
-~*  Type vholm npc to challenge Styrmir the Unkillable.      *~-
-~*  Practice duels count toward your cooldown but award      *~-
-~*  separate NPC win/loss statistics.                        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  STATISTICS                                               *~-
-~*  Wins, losses, draws, and streaks are tracked per         *~-
-~*  player.  The champion title goes to the player with      *~-
-~*  the most wins across a minimum number of fights.         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read this topic top-to-bottom once.                   *~-
-~*  2) Apply the related commands in small steps.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck this topic as your setup evolves.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Most issues come from skipped prerequisites.             *~-
-~*  If behavior differs, verify stats, toggles, resources.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-

-~*  Intro                                                    *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Welcome to the Viking Guild                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  You stand with the Vikings of 3Scapes -- a guild         *~-
-~*  built on honour, battle, craftsmanship, and the          *~-
-~*  favour of the Norse gods.                                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Your journey here is your own.  Choose a lineage,        *~-
-~*  walk a path, serve your god, and make your mark.         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  STARTING OUT                                             *~-
-~*  Type vhelp general for a guided index.                   *~-
-~*  Type vhelp commands for a full command reference.        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read this topic top-to-bottom once.                   *~-
-~*  2) Apply the related commands in small steps.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck this topic as your setup evolves.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Most issues come from skipped prerequisites.             *~-
-~*  If behavior differs, verify stats, toggles, resources.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vhelp general/intro                                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vlineage, vgod                                 *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Intro extended                                           *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Vikings Guild - Extended Introduction                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Vikings is not simply a new guild                        *~-
-~*  but a new and unique guild                               *~-
-~*  experience. It is unique in that                         *~-
-~*  it has two parallel tracks                               *~-
-~*  of advancement: the traditional                          *~-
-~*  grind to gain gxp which is                               *~-
-~*  then spent to advance guild skills                       *~-
-~*  (4 skill raises = 1 glvl)                                *~-
-~*  and, the building and development of your settlement     *~-
-~*  (think Civilization).                                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  These two tracks are linked to                           *~-
-~*  one another in the theme and                             *~-
-~*  identity of the guild and,                               *~-
-~*  share a common resource - the                            *~-
-~*  Daler. The guild has truly                               *~-
-~*  immense depth and complexity so                          *~-
-~*  it is strongly advised to read                           *~-
-~*  the many helpfiles, ask many                             *~-
-~*  questions, and to not be                                 *~-
-~*  discouraged. It takes time to take                       *~-
-~*  it all in and to get into the swing of the very many     *~-
-~*  possibilities offered. Also the guild is designed to     *~-
-~*  require little to no scripting.                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  This helpfile is designed to                             *~-
-~*  give you a deeper but by no                              *~-
-~*  means exhaustive introduction to core guild concepts.    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Your Viking                                              *~-
-~*  As detailed in "vhelp getting_started" you begin your    *~-
-~*  journey by adding depth and persona to your character.   *~-
-~*  You choose your lineage                                  *~-
-~*  (vlineage), your god (vgod), and                         *~-
-~*  your initial guild weapon (note that Vikings can only    *~-
-~*  use guild weapons).                                      *~-
-~*  You can then proceed to train your first skill, done in  *~-
-~*  the Saga Hall of the guild, and                          *~-
-~*  in setting up your spells.                               *~-
-~*  But I suggest that before doing                          *~-
-~*  that you proceed with this                               *~-
-~*  guide which explains some key concepts/features of the   *~-
-~*  guild.                                                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Daler                                                    *~-
-~*  Daler is both a measure of fame and the guild currency   *~-
-~*  gained from killing mobs (based on your glevel and not   *~-
-~*  on mob size) and by engaging in                          *~-
-~*  trade (vtrade) and acting                                *~-
-~*  like a viking by sending your longships (vlongship) to   *~-
-~*  raid.                                                    *~-
-~*  You spend daler in raising your guild skills (vtrain in  *~-
-~*  the Saga Hall of the guild)                              *~-
-~*  and in building improvements                             *~-
-~*  for your settlement (vbuild).                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Guild Skills, GXP Gain, GXP Use                          *~-
-~*  Guild skills have four distinct Vegr (paths) -           *~-
-~*  Vitka (offensive, defensive and healing spell casting)   *~-
-~*  Berserksgangr (melee offensive and defensive skills)     *~-
-~*  Hersins (guild follower skills)                          *~-
-~*  Buandi (settlement skills)                               *~-
-~*  Combat use of Vitka,                                     *~-
-~*  Berserksgangr and Hersins abilities                      *~-
-~*  will gain you gxp in the respective path which can then  *~-
-~*  be used to advance skills in each individual tree. Gxp   *~-
-~*  for the Buandi Path is automatically gained as a sort    *~-
-~*  of spillover effect from gxp                             *~-
-~*  gained in the other 3 paths.                             *~-
-~*  With the exception of the first signature skill in each  *~-
-~*  path, raising all other skills                           *~-
-~*  costs both GXP and Daler.                                *~-
-~*  You can choose to specialize in one path, and            *~-
-~*  specialization will bring benefits, but you do not need  *~-
-~*  to do it immediately. When you have made your choice,    *~-
-~*  you will need to find the appropriate NPC in the biome   *~-
-~*  (vhelp map).                                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Abilities and Spells                                     *~-
-~*  As you raise melee and follower skills you will gain     *~-
-~*  abilities which can be toggled via the vtoggle command.  *~-
-~*  With regards to spells, everyone starts with the same    *~-
-~*  rank 1 spells (vspells) and each spell is linked to one  *~-
-~*  particular god. There are 5 spell categories -           *~-
-~*  offensive, defensive, healing, enchantment and           *~-
-~*  divination.                                              *~-
-~*  Each cast of a spell increments both your knowledge in   *~-
-~*  that spell category and your devotion to the linked god  *~-
-~*  (vgod) and eventually through repeated usage you will    *~-
-~*  unlock rank 2 spells. Again, there is a small spillover  *~-
-~*  effect which slowly raises all                           *~-
-~*  devotions and categories.                                *~-
-~*  The number and category of spells you can cast each      *~-
-~*  round depend on relevant skill levels and can be set/    *~-
-~*  changed via vspells autocast.                            *~-
-~*  Lastly, the vtoggle command will allow you to            *~-
-~*  toggle a variety of abilities.                           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  The Settlement                                           *~-
-~*  Each player can found (vcity found) his own settlement   *~-
-~*  (vcity) which can then be                                *~-
-~*  expanded (vbuild). Each building                         *~-
-~*  type has a cost to build, a function, and it produces a  *~-
-~*  good and/or effect. Each building can be upgraded with   *~-
-~*  each upgrade costing progressively more resources and    *~-
-~*  daler.                                                   *~-
-~*  The resources can be sold to and/or bought from other    *~-
-~*  NPC Viking settlements (vtrade dispatch) or to other     *~-
-~*  Viking players (vtrade market). The amount you can sell  *~-
-~*  is limited by your number of carts & their capacity and  *~-
-~*  the amount you can buy is obviously also limited by      *~-
-~*  your Daler.                                              *~-
-~*  You can dedicate as little to as much time as            *~-
-~*  you want to your settlement.                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Missions and Reputation                                  *~-
-~*  There are two types of missions which can be undertaken  *~-
-~*  - newbie missions (vmission newbie) and normal missions  *~-
-~*  (vmission list).                                         *~-
-~*  Newbie missions, designed to                             *~-
-~*  help your start in Vikings,                              *~-
-~*  are the classic fetch                                    *~-
-~*  something from town A and bring to                       *~-
-~*  town B for a small reward in daler and a trade good.     *~-
-~*  Up to and until glvl 20 you                              *~-
-~*  can do 5 newbie missions per                             *~-
-~*  5 hours. Past glvl 20, you can do 3 newbie missions per  *~-
-~*  5 hours.                                                 *~-
-~*  Missions are similar in that                             *~-
-~*  you need to bring X amounts                              *~-
-~*  of one or more resources (produced in your settlement)   *~-
-~*  to an NPC Viking town and in return you will receive a   *~-
-~*  reward in Daler and an increase in faction for that      *~-
-~*  specific lineage.                                        *~-
-~*  Reputation (vrep) is important in that it influences     *~-
-~*  various guild mechanics, some obvious some not.          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Hird                                                     *~-
-~*  Hird were historically both the guards which defended    *~-
-~*  a Viking village and partook in raids and, the personal  *~-
-~*  bodyguards of the Jarls and as such, it is your task to  *~-
-~*  manage both the defense of your settlement and the       *~-
-~*  defense of your person.                                  *~-
-~*  In the case of the former, you will need to first build  *~-
-~*  a longhouse (which produces guards) and then a garrison  *~-
-~*  (which determines how many                               *~-
-~*  guards you can have stationed.                           *~-
-~*  The guards, along with your settlement's defensive       *~-
-~*  buildings, will determine how successfully you defend    *~-
-~*  yourself against raids.                                  *~-
-~*  Should you choose to raid another settlement, it will    *~-
-~*  be conducted via your longship (vlongship) which can be  *~-
-~*  upgraded making it both more seaworthy and allowing it   *~-
-~*  to carry more warriors.                                  *~-
-~*  If you choose to raid npc Viking settlements, you will   *~-
-~*  suffer a faction loss however should they raid you (and  *~-
-~*  it will occasionally happen!) you can then retaliate     *~-
-~*  against them without any faction loss.                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Ready, set, KILL!                                        *~-
-~*  Hopefully by now, you will have a slightly better idea   *~-
-~*  of the guild and will be ready to do what a mudder does  *~-
-~*  best: GRIND! But before you do that -                    *~-
-~*  1) Use vreflex to set your healing spell to fire off     *~-
-~*  at a % of your hps. It is suggested that you use the     *~-
-~*  spell "baldursljos" for this                             *~-
-~*  2) Modify your hpbar to your                             *~-
-~*  liking with the vsethp command                           *~-
-~*  3) After you slaughter a mob, you perform "vrite" on     *~-
-~*  the corpse. This will return some daler, some favour     *~-
-~*  to your patron God (and some spillover to other Gods)    *~-
-~*  and, if you vtoggle auto_scavenge you have a chance      *~-
-~*  to find some "spoils" which can be sold as a trade       *~-
-~*  good via the vtrade command.                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vhelp                                          *~-
-~*  getting_started, vlineage, vgod                          *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Lore                                                     *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Norse Lore and Setting                                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  The Viking guild draws on the mythology, history,        *~-
-~*  and culture of the Norse peoples.  The nine worlds       *~-
-~*  of Yggdrasil form the backdrop for guild lore.           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  The gods of Asgard grant power to those who seek         *~-
-~*  their favour.  The lineages trace bloodlines to          *~-
-~*  real and legendary Norse dynasties.                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Explore the help system under deities and lineage        *~-
-~*  for lore on the specific gods and houses.                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read this topic top-to-bottom once.                   *~-
-~*  2) Apply the related commands in small steps.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck this topic as your setup evolves.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Most issues come from skipped prerequisites.             *~-
-~*  If behavior differs, verify stats, toggles, resources.   *~-

-~*  Paths                                                    *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  The Four Sagas -- The Viking Paths                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Your saga accumulates across four paths.  Each           *~-
-~*  represents a different way of life and provides          *~-
-~*  a distinct range of skills to invest in.                 *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Viga         War and combat.  The warrior's path.        *~-
-~*  Vitka        Seid and magic.  The seer's path.           *~-
-~*  Hersins      Command and leadership.  The jarl's path.   *~-
-~*  Buandi       Settlement and trade.  The settler's path.  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  You can invest in all four or focus deeply on one.       *~-
-~*  Your subclass choice shapes which paths reward you       *~-
-~*  most richly.                                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read this topic top-to-bottom once.                   *~-
-~*  2) Apply the related commands in small steps.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck this topic as your setup evolves.             *~-

-~*  Quests                                                   *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Guild Quests                                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  The guild has several quests that unlock abilities       *~-
-~*  and mark milestones.  Use vquest to see your             *~-
-~*  current progress.                                        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  THE LEDUNG                                               *~-
-~*  A call to rally the north.  Requires dedication          *~-
-~*  and travel across the biome to complete.                 *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  THE VITKI'S TEACHING                                     *~-
-~*  A lesson in old knowledge from a wandering seer.         *~-
-~*  Requires some experience in the guild first.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  THE FIRST MARK                                           *~-
-~*  A rite of passage for those who have earned              *~-
-~*  standing in Midgard.  Unlocks tattoos.                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  THE WARDEN'S MARK                                        *~-
-~*  Something stirs in the ruins north of Midgard.           *~-
-~*  Orm the Brawler in Midgard knows about it.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Discovery is part of each quest.                         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
