-~*  Raids                                                    *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  The Raid System                                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Raids are organised attacks launched by longship.        *~-
-~*  A fleet is crewed with hirdmadrs and sent to a           *~-
-~*  target location in the biome.                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Success depends on your fleet strength, crew, and        *~-
-~*  the target's defenses.  Rewards include goods and        *~-
-~*  daler.                                                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Defend your own city by garrisoning hirdmadrs.           *~-
-~*  A stronger garrison discourages raid attempts.           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read this topic top-to-bottom once.                   *~-
-~*  2) Apply the related commands in small steps.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck this topic as your setup evolves.             *~-

-~*  Ranks                                                    *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Viking Guild Ranks                                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Rank is determined by your Virding (guild level).        *~-
-~*  Your title changes with your                             *~-
-~*  subclass (vhelp general/paths).                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  RANK THRESHOLDS                                          *~-
-~*  Rank 1       Virding   0.  Starting rank.                *~-
-~*  Rank 2       Virding  40.  Half a path mastered.         *~-
-~*  Rank 3       Virding  85.  One full path mastered.       *~-
-~*  Rank 4       Virding 170.  Two full paths mastered.      *~-
-~*  Rank 5       Virding 275.  Three paths mastered.         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  BERSERKER TITLES                                         *~-
-~*  Rank 1       Drengr                                      *~-
-~*  Rank 2       Berserkr                                    *~-
-~*  Rank 3       Hersir                                      *~-
-~*  Rank 4       Vikingr Fraegr                              *~-
-~*  Rank 5       Einherji                                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-

-~*  Road travel                                              *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Road Travel Between Settlements                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  To travel between Midgard, lineage villages, and         *~-
-~*  player settlements, speak to the stablemaster at         *~-
-~*  a cart stop.                                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  HOW TO START                                             *~-
-~*  1) talk stablemaster                                     *~-
-~*  2) say travel                                            *~-
-~*  3) say destinations                                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  BOOK A TRIP                                              *~-
-~*  Say the place name you want.  The stablemaster           *~-
-~*  quotes fare and travel time.                             *~-
-~*  Then say yes to take the seat, or say cancel to          *~-
-~*  stop.                                                    *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  say travel                                               *~-
-~*  say destinations                                         *~-
-~*  say midgard                                              *~-
-~*  say longholt                                             *~-
-~*  say yes                                                  *~-
-~*  say cancel                                               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  If the stablemaster does not respond, start with         *~-
-~*  talk stablemaster.                                       *~-
-~*  If your quote expired, say the destination again         *~-
-~*  for a fresh fare.                                        *~-
-~*  If your wording is unclear, say destinations and         *~-
-~*  pick one of the listed names.                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-

-~*  Rules                                                    *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Viking Guild Rules                                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  MUD RULES                                                *~-
-~*  All mud rules, as outlined in help rules, apply to       *~-
-~*  Vikings.  These are the baseline expectations for all    *~-
-~*  players and must be followed without exception.          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  QUEST RULES                                              *~-
-~*  All mud quest rules, as outlined in help quest, apply    *~-
-~*  to Vikings.  Quest integrity is essential to fair play.  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  NO QUARTER                                               *~-
-~*  Historically Vikings were fierce warriors who asked      *~-
-~*  for no quarter and gave no quarter.  If you break any    *~-
-~*  of the afore-mentioned rules, you too will be given      *~-
-~*  no quarter.                                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  BUGS AND EXPLOITS                                        *~-
-~*  The guild has been extensively play-tested to iron out   *~-
-~*  bugs and any loopholes or shortcuts which could give     *~-
-~*  an unfair advantage.  However, bugs happen and some      *~-
-~*  clever dick could potentially discover a self-serving    *~-
-~*  loophole.  If you happen to be said clever dick, report  *~-
-~*  it immediately.  Failure to do so or hiding behind some  *~-
-~*  lame excuse will result in                               *~-
-~*  your gobj being blood-eagled.                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  GUILD LINE CONDUCT                                       *~-
-~*  The guild line welcomes banter, jokes, good-natured      *~-
-~*  teasing and, of course, questions.  There is no place    *~-
-~*  nor tolerance for being rude or discriminatory in any    *~-
-~*  way.  Respect your fellow Vikings.                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  SETTLEMENT NAMING                                        *~-
-~*  In keeping with the spirit and identity of the guild,    *~-
-~*  please make an effort in appropriately naming your       *~-
-~*  settlement.  No silly names like Pineappleville or       *~-
-~*  Rictor's Neon Noobville.  Choose names that fit the      *~-
-~*  Norse theme and setting.                                 *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  ADMIN CONTACT                                            *~-
-~*  Our esteemed WGM Konungr Skuggis is often busy with      *~-
-~*  RL, coding or drinking Budweiser.  Please direct         *~-
-~*  questions or requests for aid to the player admin        *~-
-~*  before reaching out to the WGM.                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read these rules carefully before joining.            *~-
-~*  2) Follow them at all times while in the guild.          *~-
-~*  3) Report bugs and exploits immediately.                 *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vbug                                           *~-

-~*  Scavenge                                                 *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Scavenge -- Field Skill                                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  The art of finding useful items in debris and ruins.     *~-
-~*  Higher skill improves the                                *~-
-~*  quality and quantity of finds.                           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Scavenging can only be performed on corpses. Use         *~-
-~*  vscavenge on a slain enemy to search their remains       *~-
-~*  for useful items, equipment, or valuables.               *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Defeat an enemy in combat.                            *~-
-~*  2) Use vscavenge on the corpse to search it.             *~-
-~*  3) Collected goods can be sold or used.                  *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vscavenge, vskills                             *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Skald                                                    *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Gunnar Stormvoice, Wandering Skald                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  A tall, weathered man with a battered lyre and           *~-
-~*  a voice like grinding millstones. Gunnar                 *~-
-~*  Stormvoice wanders the public halls of Midgard:          *~-
-~*  the great hall, feast hall, courtyard, saga              *~-
-~*  hall, trophy hall, training grounds, and                 *~-
-~*  vestibule. He stops in each to perform a verse           *~-
-~*  before moving on.                                        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  His songs are drawn from the old battle-poems:           *~-
-~*  sagas of the gods, dirges for fallen kings,              *~-
-~*  and hymns to the Thunder God and the AllFather.          *~-
-~*  He says he only carries them -- the songs                *~-
-~*  were here long before he was.                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  You can speak with him.  He will answer, eventually.     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-

-~*  Stats                                                    *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Attributes and their Effects                             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Not all attributes serve a Viking equally.  Some         *~-
-~*  drive path advancement; others affect combat and         *~-
-~*  survival directly.  Train what matters to you.           *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  CONSTITUTION (con)                                       *~-
-~*  Each point of con raises your maximum hitpoints.         *~-
-~*  This is the most universally valuable attribute --       *~-
-~*  every Viking benefits from a higher HP ceiling.          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  DEXTERITY (dex)                                          *~-
-~*  Dex improves your physical defense.  Higher dex          *~-
-~*  means harder to hit in melee.  Worth raising for         *~-
-~*  any Viking who stands in the front line.                 *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  STRENGTH (str)                                           *~-
-~*  Str is the primary attribute for the Viga warrior        *~-
-~*  path.  Melee damage and several Viga skills scale        *~-
-~*  directly with your strength score.                       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  WISDOM (wis)                                             *~-
-~*  Wis is the primary attribute for the Seid seer           *~-
-~*  path.  Spell potency, seid pool, and vitka skill         *~-
-~*  thresholds are all driven by wisdom.                     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  CHARISMA (cha)                                           *~-
-~*  Cha is the primary attribute for the Jarl path.          *~-
-~*  Leadership capabilities, hird capacity, and jarl         *~-
-~*  skill bonuses scale with your charisma score.            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  INTELLIGENCE (int)                                       *~-
-~*  Int has no meaningful effect within the Viking           *~-
-~*  guild.  It is not a path attribute and does not          *~-
-~*  influence any guild mechanic.                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read this topic top-to-bottom once.                   *~-
-~*  2) Apply the related commands in small steps.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck this topic as your setup evolves.             *~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Subclasses                                               *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Viking Subclasses                                        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  After joining, you may choose a subclass.  This          *~-
-~*  is a permanent commitment that shapes which skill        *~-
-~*  branches grow most richly for you.                       *~-
-~*  You must be Virding 30 before a mentor will              *~-
-~*  accept you into a subclass.                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Berserker    Rage-fueled combat.  Viga-focused.          *~-
-~*  Seer         Seid and devotion.  Vitka-focused.          *~-
-~*  Jarl         Warband command.  Hersins-focused.          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  CHOOSING A SUBCLASS                                      *~-
-~*  No trainer in Midgard offers this.  Each path is         *~-
-~*  held by someone who lives outside the walls -- a         *~-
-~*  practitioner who keeps to their own ground in the        *~-
-~*  biome country.  You will need to find them.              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  They do not announce themselves.  Look for signs         *~-
-~*  in the landscape: a frozen stream in a birch ring,       *~-
-~*  standing stones older than the settlement, a high        *~-
-~*  ledge where the whole valley is visible.  Each           *~-
-~*  mentor waits in a place that reflects what they          *~-
-~*  teach.  Go out.  Look around.                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  THE RITE                                                 *~-
-~*  When you find the right person, speak with them.         *~-
-~*  They will describe the path.  If you want it, say        *~-
-~*  yes.  The commitment is immediate and permanent.         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  LEAVING A SUBCLASS                                       *~-
-~*  It is possible to abandon a subclass.  The mentor        *~-
-~*  who granted it is the one who can release you.           *~-
-~*  There is a cost: a portion of your saga is lost.         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read this topic top-to-bottom once.                   *~-
-~*  2) Apply the related commands in small steps.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck this topic as your setup evolves.             *~-

-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Threk                                                    *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Threk -- The Endurance Pool                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Threk is a passive system that softens large hits.       *~-
-~*  A qualifying blow is partly diverted into an             *~-
-~*  endurance pool rather than landing in full.  The         *~-
-~*  pool then bleeds back as HP damage each heartbeat,       *~-
-~*  spreading a spike hit over several ticks.                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  TRIGGER GATE                                             *~-
-~*  A hit qualifies if it meets your trigger threshold       *~-
-~*  (% of max HP) OR is >= 60 damage -- whichever            *~-
-~*  threshold is reached first.                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  ABSORPTION                                               *~-
-~*  A set % of each qualifying hit is soaked into            *~-
-~*  the pool.  The rest lands on you immediately.            *~-
-~*  The pool holds up to 150% of your max HP.                *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  BLEED-BACK                                               *~-
-~*  Each heartbeat a % of the pool returns as HP             *~-
-~*  damage.  Higher bleed rate = pool drains faster.         *~-
-~*  Lower = damage spread over more heartbeats.              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Use vthrek to tune trigger, absorb, and bleed.           *~-
-~*  Settings save; pool contents clear on reboot.            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read this topic top-to-bottom once.                   *~-
-~*  2) Apply the related commands in small steps.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck this topic as your setup evolves.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Most issues come from skipped prerequisites.             *~-
-~*  If behavior differs, verify stats, toggles, resources.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-
-~*  vhelp general/threk                                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vthrek, vstats                                 *~-

-~*  Training                                                 *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Training Skills                                          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Skills are trained with saga points earned through       *~-
-~*  using them in the field.  Different activities           *~-
-~*  earn different types of saga.                            *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Use vskills to see available skills and current          *~-
-~*  progress.  Use vtrain <skill> to learn one when          *~-
-~*  you have enough saga saved.                              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Some skills have prerequisites.  Check vhelp skills      *~-
-~*  for requirements before training.                        *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Training is permanent and cannot be undone.              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-

-~*  Weather                                                  *~-
-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-~*~-
-~*  Weather and Seasons                                      *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Midgard cycles through four seasons, each lasting        *~-
-~*  three real days: Spring -> Summer -> Autumn -> Winter.   *~-
-~*  Weather changes roughly every three hours within a       *~-
-~*  season.  You receive a message on season or weather      *~-
-~*  change, and every ~15 min during severe weather.         *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  WEATHER TYPES                                            *~-
-~*  Clear  Overcast  Rain  Storm  Fog  Snow  Blizzard        *~-
-~*  Each can occur at strength 1 (light) to 3 (heavy).       *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  WHAT WEATHER AFFECTS                                     *~-
-~*  City production: farms, fisheries, lumber yards,         *~-
-~*  smithies, tanneries, and breweries gain or lose          *~-
-~*  output per tick.  Spring rain boosts farms;              *~-
-~*  blizzards hurt most outdoor buildings.                   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Trade prices: storms cut fish supply; blizzards          *~-
-~*  push timber up; cold drives mead demand.                 *~-
-~*  Summer clear weather boosts grain and fish.              *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Raids: summer is peak season (more frequent,             *~-
-~*  stronger attackers).  Winter suppresses raids.           *~-
-~*  Storms delay and weaken raiders; blizzards               *~-
-~*  push the minimum raid interval out by +8 hours.          *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  Travel: biome rooms show a weather flavour line          *~-
-~*  when you move during active weather.                     *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FLOW                                              *~-
-~*  1) Read this topic top-to-bottom once.                   *~-
-~*  2) Apply the related commands in small steps.            *~-
-~*  3) Recheck this topic as your setup evolves.             *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  COMMON FAILURES                                          *~-
-~*  Most issues come from skipped prerequisites.             *~-
-~*  If behavior differs, verify stats, toggles, resources.   *~-
-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  EXAMPLES                                                 *~-

-~*                                                           *~-
-~*  See also: vbuild, vtrade                                 *~-
